# CaP-X: A Framework for Benchmarking and Improving Coding Agents for Robot Manipulation
# CaP-X：用于基准测试与改进机器人操作编程智能体的框架


Max Fu ${}^{*{12}}$ Justin Yu ${}^{*2}$ Karim El-Refai ${}^{*2}$ Ethan Kou ${}^{*2}$ Haoru Xue ${}^{*{12}}$ Huang Huang ${}^{3}$ Wenli Xiao ${}^{4}$ Guanzhi Wang ${}^{1}$ Fei-Fei Li ${}^{3}$ Guanya Shi ${}^{4}$ Jiajun Wu ${}^{3}$ Shankar Sastry ${}^{2}$ Yuke Zhu ${}^{1}$ Ken Goldberg ${}^{\dagger 2}$ Linxi "Jim" Fan ${}^{\dagger 1}$
Max Fu ${}^{*{12}}$ Justin Yu ${}^{*2}$ Karim El-Refai ${}^{*2}$ Ethan Kou ${}^{*2}$ Haoru Xue ${}^{*{12}}$ Huang Huang ${}^{3}$ Wenli Xiao ${}^{4}$ Guanzhi Wang ${}^{1}$ Fei-Fei Li ${}^{3}$ Guanya Shi ${}^{4}$ Jiajun Wu ${}^{3}$ Shankar Sastry ${}^{2}$ Yuke Zhu ${}^{1}$ Ken Goldberg ${}^{\dagger 2}$ Linxi "Jim" Fan ${}^{\dagger 1}$


## Abstract
## 摘要


"Code-as-Policy" considers how executable code can complement data-intensive Vision-Language-Action (VLA) methods, yet their effectiveness as autonomous controllers for embodied manipulation remains underexplored. We present CaP-X, an open-access framework for systematically studying Code-as-Policy agents in robot manipulation. At its core is CaP-Gym, an interactive environment in which agents control robots by synthesizing and executing programs that compose perception and control primitives. Building on this foundation, CaP-Bench evaluates frontier language and vision-language models across varying levels of abstraction, interaction, and perceptual grounding. Across 12 models, CaP-Bench reveals a consistent trend: performance improves with human-crafted abstractions but degrades as these priors are removed, exposing a dependence on designer scaffolding. At the same time, we observe that this gap can be mitigated through scaling agentic test-time computation-through multiturn interaction, structured execution feedback, visual differencing, automatic skill synthesis, and ensembled reasoning-substantially improves robustness even when agents operate over low-level primitives. These findings allow us to derive CaP-Agent0, a training-free framework that recovers human-level reliability on several manipulation tasks in simulation and on real embodiments. We further introduce CaP-RL, showing reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves success rates and transfers from simulation to real robot with minimal gap. Together, CaP-X provides a principled, open-access platform for advancing embodied coding agents.
“代码即策略”（Code-as-Policy）探讨了可执行代码如何补充数据密集型的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）方法，但其作为具身操作自主控制器的有效性尚待深入研究。我们提出了 CaP-X，这是一个用于系统性研究机器人操作中“代码即策略”智能体的开源框架。其核心是 CaP-Gym，这是一个交互式环境，智能体通过合成并执行组合了感知与控制原语的程序来控制机器人。在此基础上，CaP-Bench 在不同抽象层级、交互程度和感知基础下对前沿语言模型及视觉-语言模型进行了评估。通过对 12 个模型的测试，CaP-Bench 揭示了一个一致的趋势：性能随人工构建的抽象而提升，但随着这些先验条件的移除而下降，这暴露了智能体对设计者脚手架的依赖。同时，我们观察到通过扩展智能体测试时计算（包括多轮交互、结构化执行反馈、视觉差异分析、自动技能合成及集成推理），可以弥补这一差距，即使在智能体操作低级原语时，也能显著提高鲁棒性。这些发现使我们推导出了 CaP-Agent0，这是一个无需训练的框架，在仿真和真实机器人平台上均恢复了人类水平的可靠性。我们进一步引入了 CaP-RL，证明了带有可验证奖励的强化学习能提高成功率，并能以极小的差距实现从仿真到现实的迁移。总之，CaP-X 为推进具身编程智能体提供了一个原则性、开源的平台。


Project page: https://capgym.github.io
项目主页：https://capgym.github.io


## 1. Introduction
## 1. 引言


Robots have long been controlled through explicit programs that combine perception, geometry, planning, and feedback control (Fikes & Nilsson, 1971; Murray et al., 1994; Aeronautiques et al., 1998; Siciliano et al., 2008). As robots advanced to continuous, higher-dimensional spaces, these representations were integrated with geometric motion planning (Khatib, 1986), evolving into Hierarchical Task-and-Motion Planning (TAMP) (Kaelbling & Lozano-Pérez, 2011). These classical control paradigms achieve robustness through explicit structure: engineers manually write software that decomposes high-level goals into subtasks, composes perception and control modules, and handles failure and edge cases through explicit logic. While this offers strong interpretability and geometric precision guarantees, it has traditionally relied heavily on human ingenuity. The agent in this loop is a human expert who must manually design abstractions and anticipate corner cases, creating a scalability bottleneck that results in brittle, task-specific solutions that are difficult to generalize to open-ended environments.
长期以来，机器人一直通过显式程序进行控制，这些程序结合了感知、几何、规划和反馈控制（Fikes & Nilsson, 1971; Murray et al., 1994; Aeronautiques et al., 1998; Siciliano et al., 2008）。随着机器人向连续、更高维空间发展，这些表示方法与几何运动规划（Khatib, 1986）相结合，演变为分层任务与运动规划（TAMP）（Kaelbling & Lozano-Pérez, 2011）。这些经典控制范式通过显式结构实现鲁棒性：工程师手动编写软件，将高级目标分解为子任务，组合感知与控制模块，并通过显式逻辑处理故障和边缘情况。虽然这提供了强大的可解释性和几何精度保证，但传统上它严重依赖于人类的智慧。此循环中的智能体是人类专家，必须手动设计抽象并预判极端情况，这造成了可扩展性瓶颈，导致解决方案往往脆弱且针对特定任务，难以推广到开放式环境。


Driven by successes in data scaling for foundation models (Devlin et al., 2018; Radford et al., 2018; 2019; Brown et al., 2020; Chowdhery et al., 2023; Achiam et al., 2023; Radford et al., 2021; Li et al., 2023), another robot control paradigm has emerged in the form of Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models (Brohan et al., 2023; Kim et al., 2024; Octo Model Team et al., 2024; Jang et al., 2022; Jiang et al., 2023; Reed et al., 2022; Open X-Embodiment Collaboration et al., 2024; Shah et al., 2023; Fu et al., 2024; Huang et al., 2025; Bjorck et al., 2025; TRI LBM Team et al., 2025; Physical Intelligence et al., 2025). These approaches learn directly from large-scale visual-motor data, interpolating across massive imitation datasets to achieve impressive performance on contact-rich tasks such as shirt folding, tool use, and whole-body locomotion manipulation. However, VLAs inherit the limitations of their training data and design: they often lack interpretability and struggle to generalize to new robot embodiments and novel long-horizon tasks without additional data collection and retraining. Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) suggest a way to bridge these paradigms: using general-purpose coding agents to replace the human engineer in the programmatic control loop. Modern coding agents have demonstrated the ability to synthesize executable code, define functions, and debug failures on software benchmarks such as SWE-Bench (Jimenez et al., 2024). Unlike earlier language-conditioned planners limited to function calling (Tellex et al., 2011), today's agents can construct mid- to low-level logic that closely resembles expert code. However, while Code-as-Policy (CaP) pioneers (Liang et al., 2023; Singh et al., 2023) validated this approach in applications to robotics, they mostly rely on high-level primitives (e.g., stack_objs_in_order ()) that offer significant task-specific simplifications. As a result, it remains unclear how much of the observed performance in robot control stems from the agent itself versus the structure imposed by these primitives. In particular, prior work does not systematically characterize how agent performance changes as such scaffolding is reduced, nor to what extent increased test-time computation-through iterative debugging, skill synthesis, ensembled reasoning, or multimodal grounding—can compensate for operating over lower-level interfaces.
受基础模型数据规模化成功（Devlin et al., 2018; Radford et al., 2018; 2019; Brown et al., 2020; Chowdhery et al., 2023; Achiam et al., 2023; Radford et al., 2021; Li et al., 2023）的推动，另一种机器人控制范式——视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型应运而生（Brohan et al., 2023; Kim et al., 2024; Octo Model Team et al., 2024; Jang et al., 2022; Jiang et al., 2023; Reed et al., 2022; Open X-Embodiment Collaboration et al., 2024; Shah et al., 2023; Fu et al., 2024; Huang et al., 2025; Bjorck et al., 2025; TRI LBM Team et al., 2025; Physical Intelligence et al., 2025）。这些方法直接从大规模视觉-运动数据中学习，通过对海量模仿数据集进行插值，在折叠衣物、工具使用和全身运动操作等接触密集型任务中表现出色。然而，VLA模型继承了其训练数据和设计上的局限性：它们往往缺乏可解释性，且在没有额外数据收集和重训练的情况下，难以泛化到新的机器人形态和新颖的长程任务中。大语言模型（LLM）的最新进展提供了一种弥合这些范式的方法：利用通用编程智能体取代程序控制循环中的人类工程师。现代编程智能体已证明能够合成可执行代码、定义函数并在SWE-Bench等软件基准测试中调试故障（Jimenez et al., 2024）。与早期局限于函数调用的语言条件规划器（Tellex et al., 2011）不同，如今的智能体能够构建与专家代码高度相似的中低层逻辑。然而，尽管“代码即策略”（CaP）的先驱者（Liang et al., 2023; Singh et al., 2023）在机器人应用中验证了该方法，但他们主要依赖于提供显著任务特定简化的顶层原语（例如 stack_objs_in_order()）。因此，目前尚不清楚机器人控制中观察到的性能有多少源于智能体本身，又有多少源于这些原语所施加的结构。特别是，现有工作尚未系统地表征当这种脚手架减少时智能体性能如何变化，也未探讨增加测试时计算（通过迭代调试、技能合成、集成推理或多模态接地）在多大程度上可以补偿在更低层接口上操作带来的挑战。

Figure 1. (Top) CaP-Bench Task Success Rate over Model Release Date: We primarily compare 7 tasks over 12 models' task success rates resulting from model-generated code against those from human experts. We find that while (vision-) language models have achieved capabilities comparable to humans in other domains (Jimenez et al., 2024; Rein et al., 2024; Hendrycks et al., 2020), they still trail behind human performance in generating programmatic robot control code for diverse manipulation tasks in simulation and in the real world. (Bottom): CaP-Gym integrates RoboSuite (Zhu et al., 2020), LIBERO-PRO (Zhou et al., 2025), and BEHAVIOR (Li et al., 2024a). We further present CaP-Agent0 (Section 4), a training-free agentic framework that recovers near human-level performance on several manipulation tasks and achieves success rates comparable to- and in some cases exceeding-those of post-trained VLAs, without any task-specific training data.
图1.（上）CaP-Bench任务成功率随模型发布时间的变化：我们主要比较了12个模型在7项任务中的成功率，对比了模型生成的代码与人类专家代码的表现。我们发现，尽管（视觉-）语言模型在其他领域已达到与人类相当的能力（Jimenez et al., 2024; Rein et al., 2024; Hendrycks et al., 2020），但在为仿真和现实世界中多样化操作任务生成程序化机器人控制代码方面，它们仍落后于人类表现。（下）：CaP-Gym集成了RoboSuite（Zhu et al., 2020）、LIBERO-PRO（Zhou et al., 2025）和BEHAVIOR（Li et al., 2024a）。我们进一步提出了CaP-Agent0（第4节），这是一个无需训练的智能体框架，在多个操作任务上恢复了接近人类水平的性能，且在无需任何任务特定训练数据的情况下，实现了与后训练VLA相当、甚至在某些情况下超过其表现的成功率。


To address this gap, we introduce CaP-X, a unified framework for systematically evaluating and improving code-based robot control agents. At the core of CaP-X is CaP-Gym, an interactive environment in which agents directly control robots by generating and executing programs that compose perception and control primitives. CaP-Gym integrates 187 tasks from standard robot manipulation simulators—including RoboSuite (Zhu et al., 2020), LIBERO-PRO (Liu et al., 2023b; Zhou et al., 2025), and BEHAVIOR (Li et al., 2024a)-under a shared primitive design that is intentionally compatible with both simulation and physical robot systems.
为了解决这一差距，我们引入了CaP-X，这是一个用于系统评估和改进基于代码的机器人控制智能体的统一框架。CaP-X的核心是CaP-Gym，这是一个交互式环境，智能体通过生成和执行组合了感知与控制原语的程序来直接控制机器人。CaP-Gym集成了来自标准机器人操作模拟器的187项任务——包括RoboSuite（Zhu et al., 2020）、LIBERO-PRO（Liu et al., 2023b; Zhou et al., 2025）和BEHAVIOR（Li et al., 2024a）——并采用了在仿真和物理机器人系统上均兼容的统一原语设计。


Building on CaP-Gym, we construct CaP-Bench, a benchmark designed to systematically study agentic capability along three axes: Abstraction Level: Varying the action space from human-crafted macros (High-Level) to atomic, fundamental primitives (Low-Level); Temporal Interaction: Comparing zero-shot single-turn program generation against multi-turn interaction to quantify capabilities in failure recovery and iterative reasoning; and Perceptual Grounding: Evaluating how different modalities of visual feedback impact the agent's ability to ground task-relevant visual features into code generation. We instantiate CaP-Bench by focusing on a subset of 7 environments from CaP-Gym and evaluate 12 state-of-the-art open- and closed-source language models and vision-language models.
基于 CaP-Gym，我们构建了 CaP-Bench，这是一个旨在从三个维度系统研究智能体能力的基准：抽象级别：改变动作空间，从人工编写的宏指令（高层）到原子级的基本原语（底层）；时间交互：比较零样本单轮程序生成与多轮交互，以量化其在故障恢复和迭代推理方面的能力；以及感知基础：评估不同视觉反馈模态如何影响智能体将任务相关视觉特征转化为代码生成的能力。我们通过聚焦 CaP-Gym 中 7 个环境的子集来实例化 CaP-Bench，并评估了 12 个最先进的开源和闭源语言模型及视觉语言模型。


Guided by insights from CaP-Bench results, we derive CaP-Agent0, a training-free agentic framework that augments coding models with multi-turn interaction, visual grounding into text, an automatically synthesized task-agnostic skill library, and parallelized multi-model code generation. CaP-Agent0 achieves performance comparable to, and in some cases exceeding, human expert baselines on CaP-Bench tasks. Finally, we show that CaP-Gym supports CaP-RL-reinforcement learning on the coding agent itself. On-policy post-training with environment rewards improves task success, while synthesized programs transfer directly to real robots. This paper makes the following contributions:
在 CaP-Bench 结果的启发下，我们推导出了 CaP-Agent0，这是一个无需训练的智能体框架，通过多轮交互、视觉到文本的接地、自动合成的任务无关技能库以及并行多模型代码生成来增强编码模型。CaP-Agent0 在 CaP-Bench 任务上实现了与人类专家基准相当甚至在某些情况下超越的表现。最后，我们展示了 CaP-Gym 支持对编码智能体本身进行 CaP-RL 强化学习。利用环境奖励进行的策略内后训练提高了任务成功率，同时合成程序可直接迁移至真实机器人。本文做出以下贡献：


1. CaP-Gym, a unified suite of interactive robot coding environments spanning tabletop, bimanual, and mobile manipulation tasks, designed for evaluating and training code-generating multimodal embodied agents.
1. CaP-Gym，一套统一的交互式机器人编码环境，涵盖桌面、双臂及移动操作任务，专为评估和训练生成代码的多模态具身智能体而设计。

2. CaP-Bench, a systematic benchmark that measures robot control performance across tasks and levels of primitives and modalities.
2. CaP-Bench，一个系统化的基准测试，用于衡量机器人控制在不同任务、原语级别和模态下的性能。


3. Two approaches to improving performance: CaP-Agent0, a training-free, agentic scaffolding approach comprising a combination of multi-turn visual differencing, ensembled reasoning, and automatic skill library synthesis; CaP-RL, reinforcement learning on the coding agent via environment reward.
3. 两种提升性能的方法：CaP-Agent0，一种无需训练的智能体脚手架方法，结合了多轮视觉差异分析、集成推理和自动技能库合成；CaP-RL，通过环境奖励对编码智能体进行强化学习。


## 2. CaP-Gym
## 2. CaP-Gym


CaP-Gym is a hierarchical control framework built on the standard Gymnasium interface (Brockman et al., 2016). It binds a Low-Level Environment loop (a physics simulator or the real world) with a stateful Code Executor loop. Architecturally, CaP-Gym preserves the native dynamics of underlying simulators, e.g., Robosuite (Zhu et al., 2020), LIBERO-PRO (Liu et al., 2023b; Zhou et al., 2025), and BEHAVIOR (Li et al., 2024a), while exposing them through a Read-Eval-Print Loop (REPL) paradigm tailored for coding agents. In this design, a single code environment "turn" corresponds to the full execution of a generated code program, which may trigger multiple underlying simulation steps depending on the logics invoked.
CaP-Gym 是一个构建在标准 Gymnasium 接口（Brockman et al., 2016）之上的分层控制框架。它将低级环境循环（物理模拟器或真实世界）与有状态的代码执行器循环绑定。在架构上，CaP-Gym 保留了底层模拟器（如 Robosuite (Zhu et al., 2020)、LIBERO-PRO (Liu et al., 2023b; Zhou et al., 2025) 和 BEHAVIOR (Li et al., 2024a)）的原生动力学，同时通过专为编码智能体设计的读取-求值-输出循环（REPL）范式将其暴露出来。在此设计中，一个代码环境“轮次”对应于生成代码程序的完整执行，根据所调用的逻辑，这可能会触发多次底层模拟步骤。


### 2.1. Low-Level Perception and Control Primitives
### 2.1. 低级感知与控制原语


All computationally intensive perception and control primitives are implemented as stateless services (Christie et al., 2025), enabling high-throughput parallel evaluation.
所有计算密集型的感知与控制原语均实现为无状态服务（Christie et al., 2025），从而支持高吞吐量的并行评估。


Perception Primitives Agents access perceptual data from the environment through modular perception primitives that abstract raw sensor data into structured semantic objects, e.g., SAM3 (Carion et al., 2025) for language-conditioned segmentation and Molmo 2 (Clark et al., 2026) for open-vocabulary pointing, alongside standard vision libraries like
感知原语 智能体通过模块化感知原语从环境中获取感知数据，这些原语将原始传感器数据抽象为结构化的语义对象，例如用于语言条件分割的 SAM3 (Carion et al., 2025) 和用于开放词汇指点的 Molmo 2 (Clark et al., 2026)，以及标准的视觉库，如


OpenCV (Bradski, 2000) and Open3D (Zhou et al., 2018).
OpenCV (Bradski, 2000) 和 Open3D (Zhou et al., 2018)。


Control Primitives Instead of directly emitting joint-space action commands, agents call motion planners or inverse kinematics solvers such as PyRoki (Kim et al., 2025). They can handle collision checking, reachability constraints, and action-space transformations, allowing agents to reason in a task-oriented Cartesian space while delegating execution feasibility to the controller.
控制原语 智能体不直接发出关节空间动作指令，而是调用运动规划器或逆运动学求解器，例如 PyRoki (Kim et al., 2025)。它们可以处理碰撞检测、可达性约束和动作空间转换，使智能体能够在面向任务的笛卡尔空间中进行推理，同时将执行可行性委托给控制器。


## 3. CaP-Bench: Evaluating Frontier Models
## 3. CaP-Bench：评估前沿模型


Models. We evaluate 12 state-of-the-art vision-language and language models, including closed-source frontier models (Gemini-3-Pro (Google DeepMind, 2025), OpenAI GPT o1 (OpenAI, 2024), o4-mini (OpenAI, 2025d), 5.1 (OpenAI, 2025a) and 5.2 (OpenAI, 2025b), and Claude Haiku 4.5 (Anthropic, 2025a) and Opus 4.5 (Anthropic, 2025b), and open source models (OpenAI GPT-OSS-20B and 120B (OpenAI, 2025c), Qwen3 235B (QwenLM / Alibaba Cloud, 2025), Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct, Kimi K2 Instruct (AI, 2025), and DeepSeek-V3.1-Terminus (DeepSeek-AI, 2024)).
模型。我们评估了 12 个最先进的视觉语言模型和语言模型，包括闭源前沿模型（Gemini-3-Pro (Google DeepMind, 2025)、OpenAI GPT o1 (OpenAI, 2024)、o4-mini (OpenAI, 2025d)、5.1 (OpenAI, 2025a) 和 5.2 (OpenAI, 2025b)，以及 Claude Haiku 4.5 (Anthropic, 2025a) 和 Opus 4.5 (Anthropic, 2025b)）以及开源模型（OpenAI GPT-OSS-20B 和 120B (OpenAI, 2025c)、Qwen3 235B (QwenLM / Alibaba Cloud, 2025)、Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct、Kimi K2 Instruct (AI, 2025) 和 DeepSeek-V3.1-Terminus (DeepSeek-AI, 2024)）。


Task Suite. Primary analysis is performed across 7 core tasks ranging from single-arm manipulation to bimanual coordination: Cube Lift, Cube Stack, Spill Wipe, Peg Insertion, Cube Re-stack, Two-Arm Lift, and Two-Arm Handover. Each task is evaluated with 100 trials per tier. In Section 4, we further extend this analysis to diverse long-horizon settings using tasks from LIBERO-PRO (Zhou et al., 2025) and BEHAVIOR (Li et al., 2024a) (see Section 4).
任务套件。主要分析涵盖了从单臂操作到双臂协作的 7 个核心任务：立方体提升、立方体堆叠、溢出擦除、插销插入、立方体重新堆叠、双臂提升和双臂交接。每个任务在每个层级下均进行 100 次试验评估。在第 4 节中，我们利用 LIBERO-PRO (Zhou et al., 2025) 和 BEHAVIOR (Li et al., 2024a) 中的任务，将此分析进一步扩展到多样化的长程场景（见第 4 节）。


Protocol. We evaluate models using a Zero-Shot Pass@1 protocol. Within a trial, agents may interact with the environment over one or multiple turns, observing execution feedback and generating subsequent code to recover from errors or extract additional information; the environment is never reset during the trial. Unlike evaluation settings that permit retries through environment resets, each task instance allows only one continuous interaction episode. Coding agent task performance is compared against that of human expert-written reference solutions under identical environments and primitives. We introduce 4 single-turn tiers (S1-S4) and 4 multi-turn tiers (M1-M4) to CaP-Bench. Please refer to Table 1 for a tabular comparison.
协议。我们使用零样本 Pass@1 协议评估模型。在一次试验中，智能体可以在一轮或多轮中与环境交互，观察执行反馈并生成后续代码以从错误中恢复或提取额外信息；试验期间环境从不重置。与允许通过环境重置进行重试的评估设置不同，每个任务实例仅允许一次连续的交互片段。编码智能体的任务性能与相同环境和原语下人类专家编写的参考解决方案进行对比。我们在 CaP-Bench 中引入了 4 个单轮层级（S1-S4）和 4 个多轮层级（M1-M4）。请参阅表 1 获取表格对比。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_3.jpg?x=158&y=189&w=1439&h=777&r=0"/>



Figure 2. (Left) An example of code generated by Gemini-3-Pro for completing the task "lift the red cube" using the high-level primitives. (Right) Code generated by Gemini-3-Pro using just low-level primitives to achieve the same functionality as a single high-level primitive. For more details on the differences between high and low-level primitives, see Section 3.1 and Appendix F.
图 2。（左）Gemini-3-Pro 使用高层原语完成“抬起红色方块”任务生成的代码示例。（右）Gemini-3-Pro 仅使用底层原语实现与单个高层原语相同功能所生成的代码。关于高层与底层原语区别的更多详情，请参阅第 3.1 节和附录 F。


### 3.1. Single-Turn Benchmarks (S1-S4)
### 3.1. 单轮基准测试 (S1-S4)


High-Level (S1 & S2): These tiers evaluate the agent's ability to reason with human-designed primitives. We evaluate this in two modes: Privileged (S1), which uses ground-truth simulation state (masks and object poses), and NonPrivileged (S2), which relies on real perception modules processing raw RGB-D inputs-the default setting for most prior work. We introduce S1 to disentangle high-level planning from perception noise, establishing a reasoning upper bound that allows us to distinguish between algorithmic failures and visual estimation errors.
高层 (S1 & S2)：这些层级旨在评估智能体利用人类设计原语进行推理的能力。我们通过两种模式进行评估：特权模式 (S1)，使用真值模拟状态（掩码和物体位姿）；非特权模式 (S2)，依赖处理原始 RGB-D 输入的真实感知模块——这是大多数先前工作的默认设置。我们引入 S1 是为了将高层规划与感知噪声解耦，建立一个推理上限，从而区分算法故障与视觉估计误差。


Low-Level (S3 & S4): In these tiers, human-designed abstractions are replaced by their constituent low-level primitives (e.g., solve_ik (), sam3_text_prompt ()), drawn directly from the APIs of each underlying package-reflecting the interfaces that human developers use to control robots. We evaluate two settings: (S3), where documentation includes usage examples to scaffold low-level composition, and (S4), where examples are removed and the agent must reason about program structure solely from interface definitions (function signatures and docstrings). See Figure 2 for an illustration of high-level (S1 & S2) versus low-level (S3 & S4) primitives; full API details at each abstraction level are provided in Appendix F.
底层 (S3 & S4)：在这些层级中，人类设计的抽象被其构成的底层原语（例如 solve_ik()、sam3_text_prompt()）所取代，这些原语直接取自各底层包的 API，反映了人类开发者控制机器人时使用的接口。我们评估两种设置：(S3) 文档包含用于辅助底层组合的使用示例；(S4) 移除示例，智能体必须仅根据接口定义（函数签名和文档字符串）来推断程序结构。高层 (S1 & S2) 与底层 (S3 & S4) 原语的对比请见图 2；各抽象级别的完整 API 详情请见附录 F。


### 3.2. Multi-turn Benchmarks (M1-M4)
### 3.2. 多轮基准测试 (M1-M4)


Text-Only Multi-turn (M1): In this setting, the agent receives the standard output (stdout) and error traces (stderr) from the Python sandbox after each execution turn. This enables a state introspection loop: agents can proactively inject diagnostic print statements to surface hidden symbolic variables (e.g., perception estimates) and utilize these traces to diagnose logical failures and refine code without access to visual ground truth. All other multiturn tiers (M2-M4) retain access to these code execution traces.
纯文本多轮 (M1)：在此设置下，智能体在每一轮执行后都会接收来自 Python 沙箱的标准输出 (stdout) 和错误追踪 (stderr)。这实现了一个状态自省循环：智能体可以主动插入诊断性打印语句来显示隐藏的符号变量（如感知估计值），并利用这些追踪信息诊断逻辑错误并优化代码，而无需访问视觉真值。所有其他多轮层级 (M2-M4) 均保留对这些代码执行追踪的访问权限。


Multimodal (M2): The environment pipes the current RGB observation back into the agent's context window. The M2 tier is only available to multimodal foundation models that accept raw RGB images as input.
多模态 (M2)：环境将当前的 RGB 观测结果回传至智能体的上下文窗口。M2 层级仅适用于接受原始 RGB 图像作为输入的多模态基础模型。


Visual Differencing Module (M3): We introduce the Visual Differencing Module (VDM), which uses a vision-language model to convert visual observations into structured natural language. VDM is provided with the task instruction alongside visual observations. In the first turn, it generates a scene description and extracts task-relevant visual attributes. In subsequent turns, it explicitly describes differences between the previous and current image observations and whether the coding agent has completed the task. The resulting text from the VDM is provided as part of the coding agent's observation context for code generation.
视觉差异模块 (M3)：我们引入了视觉差异模块 (VDM)，它利用视觉语言模型将视觉观测转换为结构化的自然语言。VDM 在接收视觉观测的同时也会接收任务指令。在第一轮中，它生成场景描述并提取与任务相关的视觉属性。在后续轮次中，它会明确描述前后图像观测之间的差异，以及编码智能体是否已完成任务。VDM 生成的文本将作为编码智能体代码生成观测上下文的一部分提供。


Low-Level with VDM (M4): This tier has the same VDM as tier M3 and has access to the same low-level primitives and in-context usage examples as tier S3.
带 VDM 的底层测试 (M4)：该层级具备与 M3 相同的 VDM，并拥有与 S3 层级相同的底层原语和上下文内使用示例。


### 3.3. Discussion
### 3.3. 讨论


Takeaway 1: A Significant Gap Persists Between Frontier Models and Human Experts in Single-Turn Evaluation. We benchmark open- and closed-source agents against human expert solutions under an identical set of perception and control primitives in a single-turn, zero-shot setting (S4). As shown in Figure 1, while closed-source models consistently outperform open-source alternatives and newer architectures exhibit stronger capabilities, none yet match the success rate of human-crafted programs in a zero-shot Pass@1 setting.
要点 1：在单轮评估中，前沿模型与人类专家之间仍存在显著差距。我们在单轮零样本设置 (S4) 下，针对相同的一组感知和控制原语，对开源和闭源智能体与人类专家解决方案进行了基准测试。如图 1 所示，尽管闭源模型始终优于开源替代方案，且较新的架构展现出更强的能力，但在零样本 Pass@1 设置下，尚无模型能达到人类编写程序的成功率。


Takeaway 2: High-Level Abstractions Boost Performance but Limit Expressivity. Figure 3 shows a monotonic increase in task success as primitive abstraction increases, mirroring how prior Code-as-Policies (Liang et al., 2023) approaches relying on high-level primitives report strong zero-shot performance. By collapsing low-level perception, geometric reasoning, and control into human-designed primitives, these abstractions reduce the effective search space and allow models to focus on task sequencing.
要点 2：高层抽象提升了性能，但限制了表达能力。图 3 显示，随着原语抽象程度的提高，任务成功率呈单调上升趋势，这与先前依赖高层原语的“代码即策略”（Liang et al., 2023）方法报告的强劲零样本性能相呼应。通过将底层感知、几何推理和控制合并为人类设计的原语，这些抽象减少了有效的搜索空间，使模型能够专注于任务序列的规划。


However, this gain comes at the cost of expressivity. As abstraction increases, the agent's action space is increasingly constrained by human priors, imposing a generality ceiling that masks failures in low-level reasoning. In contrast, performance degradation at lower abstraction levels (S3/S4) reflects the difficulty of code synthesis, while enabling expressive behaviors—such as hierarchical perception fallback strategies (Appendix Section E.2.2)—that cannot be represented by fixed high-level primitives.
然而，这种收益是以牺牲表达能力为代价的。随着抽象程度的提高，智能体的动作空间受到人类先验的更多约束，从而设定了一个通用性上限，掩盖了底层推理中的失败。相比之下，较低抽象级别 (S3/S4) 的性能下降反映了代码合成的难度，同时也实现了更具表达力的行为——例如分层感知回退策略（附录 E.2.2 节）——这些行为是固定的高层原语所无法表示的。


This observation motivates a scalable middle ground: rather than relying on human-designed abstractions, agents should be able to recover structure from low-level primitives themselves. In Section 4, we demonstrate this capability by enabling agents to distill successful execution traces into a reusable skill library. Consequently, we propose that generalist embodied coding agents be evaluated primarily on primitive-level performance, ensuring that success stems from robust reasoning rather than from the inductive biases of an over-engineered, often task-specific, API set.
这一观察促使我们寻找一种可扩展的折中方案：与其依赖人工设计的抽象，不如让智能体能够自行从底层原语中恢复结构。在第 4 节中，我们通过使智能体能够将成功的执行轨迹提炼为可重用的技能库，展示了这一能力。因此，我们建议通用具身编码智能体应主要根据原语级性能进行评估，以确保其成功源于稳健的推理，而非过度工程化且往往针对特定任务的 API 集所带来的归纳偏置。


Takeaway 3: Closing the Loop with Multi-turn and Visual Grounding Improves Performance. We study how multi-turn interaction and different forms of visual grounding mitigate the performance gaps identified in Takeaways 1 and 2.
要点 3：通过多轮交互和视觉定位闭环可提升性能。我们研究了多轮交互和不同形式的视觉定位如何缓解要点 1 和 2 中发现的性能差距。


Allowing agents to iterate and inspect their own execution traces (st dout/st derr, M1) consistently improves performance across all models (Figure 5), highlighting the importance of explicit execution feedback for debugging
允许智能体迭代并检查其自身的执行轨迹（标准输出/标准错误，M1）在所有模型中均能持续提升性能（图 5），这凸显了显式执行反馈对于调试的重要性。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_4.jpg?x=931&y=199&w=631&h=315&r=0"/>



Figure 3. Average task success rate across open-source and closed-source models as primitive abstraction increases. As primitive abstraction increases S4 (per model performance illustrated in Figure 1) to S1 (high level primitives with full state observation), the success rate increases. This can only in part be attributed to reduced code correctness at S3-S4, see Figure 4.
图 3. 随着原语抽象程度的提高，开源和闭源模型的平均任务成功率。随着原语抽象程度从 S4（各模型性能见图 1）提高到 S1（具有完整状态观测的高级原语），成功率随之上升。这仅能部分归因于 S3-S4 阶段代码正确性的降低，详见图 4。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_4.jpg?x=931&y=757&w=628&h=327&r=0"/>



Figure 4. Code Execution Success Rate vs primitive abstraction. and recovery.
图 4. 代码执行成功率与原语抽象程度及恢复能力的关系。


Counter-intuitively, directly interleaving raw RGB observations at each turn (M2) degrades performance relative to the text-only M1 baseline. We hypothesize this degradation is due to a cross-modal alignment gap: foundation models are rarely trained to jointly reason over software coding and images of physical task execution, making raw visual inputs difficult to integrate effectively during code synthesis.
反直觉的是，在每一轮中直接交错输入原始 RGB 观测值（M2）会降低性能，表现逊于仅文本的 M1 基线。我们推测这种下降是由于跨模态对齐差距所致：基础模型很少接受过同时针对软件编码和物理任务执行图像的联合推理训练，这使得原始视觉输入在代码合成过程中难以被有效整合。


Prior work (Hu et al., 2025; Wang et al., 2026) similarly observes that textually grounded feedback outperforms raw images, though primarily in structured environments with native text states. In contrast, robotic manipulation operates in unstructured, continuous settings without ground-truth textual descriptions. Here, the Visual Differencing Module (M3) bridges this gap by converting visual observations into structured natural language, substantially outperforming both naive image interleaving (M2) and execution-only feedback (M1) across all tasks (Figure 5).
先前的工作（Hu et al., 2025; Wang et al., 2026）同样观察到，基于文本的反馈优于原始图像，但这主要是在具有原生文本状态的结构化环境中。相比之下，机器人操作是在非结构化的连续环境中进行的，且缺乏真值文本描述。在此，视觉差异模块（M3）通过将视觉观测转换为结构化自然语言弥补了这一差距，在所有任务中均显著优于简单的图像交错（M2）和仅执行反馈（M1）（图 5）。


Low-Level Primitives with Multi-turn Feedback (M4). Figure 6 shows that agents operating over low-level primitives augmented with multi-turn feedback not only surpass high-level single-turn (S2) but can reach parity with high-level multi-turn performance (M3). This supports a test-time compute scaling hypothesis: robustness can be synthesized at runtime by increasing an agent's capacity for reasoning, verification, and self-correction over atomic primitives.
具有多轮反馈的底层原语（M4）。图 6 显示，在辅以多轮反馈的底层原语上运行的智能体，不仅超越了高级单轮（S2）性能，甚至能达到与高级多轮性能（M3）相当的水平。这支持了测试时计算扩展假设：通过提高智能体在原子原语上的推理、验证和自我纠错能力，可以在运行时合成稳健性。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_5.jpg?x=173&y=191&w=658&h=245&r=0"/>



Figure 5. Comparison of single-turn (S2) and multi-turn tiers (M1- M3) across models. Enabling textual feedback through multi-turn (M1) improves task success rate in most models. Direct multimodal (M2) visual grounding reduced task success rate. We find that visual differencing into text (M3) instead of direct multimodal visual input consistently improves task success rate across both close and open source models.
图 5. 各模型单轮（S2）与多轮（M1-M3）层级的对比。通过多轮（M1）启用文本反馈提高了大多数模型的任务成功率。直接多模态（M2）视觉定位降低了任务成功率。我们发现，将视觉差异化为文本（M3）而非直接输入多模态视觉信息，在闭源和开源模型中均能持续提升任务成功率。


Across all multi-turn settings (M1-M4), both coding errors (e.g., exceptions) and physical execution failures (e.g., unstable grasps) are frequently recoverable through iterative interaction. In the absence of explicit visual grounding mechanisms (M1), successful agents compensate by proac-tively instrumenting perception primitives to expose symbolic state-such as object poses-and performing explicit checks for task completion (e.g., verifying relative object heights to confirm stacking). Visual grounding (M2-M4) reduces the burden of such self-instrumentation but does not eliminate explicit state verification behavior through perception primitives. Instead, the strongest performance emerges when agents combine structured feedback with iterative reasoning, framing multi-turn interaction as a mechanism for hypothesis testing and error recovery in embodied control.
在所有多轮设置（M1-M4）中，编码错误（如异常）和物理执行失败（如抓取不稳定）通常都可以通过迭代交互来恢复。在缺乏显式视觉定位机制（M1）的情况下，成功的智能体会主动通过感知原语来暴露符号状态（如物体位姿）并执行显式的任务完成检查（如验证物体相对高度以确认堆叠）来进行补偿。视觉定位（M2-M4）减轻了这种自检测的负担，但并未消除通过感知原语进行显式状态验证的行为。相反，当智能体将结构化反馈与迭代推理相结合，并将多轮交互视为具身控制中假设检验和错误恢复的机制时，才会产生最强的性能。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_5.jpg?x=173&y=1220&w=662&h=194&r=0"/>



Figure 6. Evaluation of Gemini-3-Pro across four tiers of the benchmark. Multi-turn with visual differencing and low-level API (M4) significantly outperforms both single-turn low-level API (S3), and more notably, single-turn high-level API (S2).
图 6. Gemini-3-Pro 在四个基准层级上的评估。具有视觉差异和底层 API 的多轮交互（M4）显著优于单轮底层 API（S3），更值得注意的是，也优于单轮高级 API（S2）。


## 4. CaP-Agent0: An Agentic Framework for Robot Control
## 4. CaP-Agent0：一种用于机器人控制的智能体框架


Based on the failure modes and insights identified in CaP-Bench, we introduce CaP-Agent0, a training-free, agentic infrastructure for robot control that augments base foundation models with a specialized multi-turn reasoning loop and a dynamically synthesized skill library. The architecture of CaP-Agent0 is designed directly to address three key gaps identified in the benchmark. We demonstrate the efficacy of each design choice in CaP-Agent0 by running ablation studies using the most capable model identified from CaP-Bench (Gemini-3-Pro) bootstrapped with each design choice, shown in Figure 8. A visual walkthrough of the agentic framework is presented in Figure 7.
基于在 CaP-Bench 中发现的故障模式和见解，我们引入了 CaP-Agent0，这是一种无需训练的机器人控制智能体基础设施，它通过专门的多轮推理循环和动态合成的技能库增强了基础模型。CaP-Agent0 的架构旨在直接解决基准测试中发现的三个关键差距。我们通过使用从 CaP-Bench 中确定的最强模型（Gemini-3-Pro）并结合各项设计选择进行消融研究，证明了 CaP-Agent0 中每项设计的有效性，如图 8 所示。图 7 展示了该智能体框架的视觉流程。


1. Multi-turn Visual Differencing (VDM): Directly adopting the insights from Takeaway 3, CaP-Agent0 integrates the Visual Differencing Module as part of the per-turn observation. By grounding observations in structured text rather than raw pixels, the agent mitigates the specific cross-modal alignment failures identified in the M2 tier.
1. 多轮视觉差异模块（VDM）：直接采纳要点 3 的见解，CaP-Agent0 将视觉差异模块整合为每轮观测的一部分。通过将观测结果基于结构化文本而非原始像素进行接地（grounding），该智能体缓解了 M2 层级中识别出的特定跨模态对齐失败问题。


2. Auto-Synthesized and Persistent Skill Libraries: In analyzing low-level S3 and S4 code generations from CaP-Bench, we found that capable models routinely synthesize auxiliary utility functions to perform robotics data manipulations.
2. 自动合成且持久化的技能库：在分析 CaP-Bench 中生成的底层 S3 和 S4 代码时，我们发现能力较强的模型会例行合成辅助工具函数，以执行机器人数据操作。


Motivated by agentic systems that accumulate reusable tools over time (Wang et al., 2023a), CaP-Agent0 introduces an automatically synthesized, task-agnostic skill library that persists across trials. Rather than requiring the agent to repeatedly re-derive low-level utilities, the library onboards commonly recurring implementation patterns and offloads fragile low-level logic, allowing the coding agent to focus on high-level semantic planning. Importantly, unlike fixed human-designed high-level APIs, these skills are discovered: they emerge from successful executions and retain the expressivity of low-level interfaces while improving robustness through reuse.
受那些随时间积累可重用工具的智能体系统（Wang et al., 2023a）启发，CaP-Agent0 引入了一个跨试验持久存在的、任务无关的自动合成技能库。该库无需智能体重复推导底层工具，而是吸纳了常见的实现模式并卸载了脆弱的底层逻辑，使编码智能体能够专注于高层语义规划。重要的是，与固定的人工设计高层 API 不同，这些技能是发现式的：它们源于成功的执行，在通过重用提高鲁棒性的同时，保留了底层接口的表达能力。


The library is constructed via an automated synthesis pipeline that can be executed by the agent itself. Code outputs from successful rollouts in tier S3 are collected, and function definitions are extracted using regular-expression matching. An LLM is then queried to perform an analysis over these extracted functions to identify frequently recurring, task-agnostic logic, which is isolated and promoted into reusable skills. While the current implementation performs a single synthesis pass, the process is inherently iterative. As additional successful executions are accumulated, the agent can continue to bootstrap, refine, or prune its skill library over time. Furthermore, depending on the desired generality, researchers can modulate the filtering leniency to allow for more task-specific behaviors or maintain a strictly task-agnostic core. A complete list of the nine synthesized functions currently utilized by CaP-Agent0 is provided in Appendix G.1.
该库通过智能体自身可执行的自动化合成流水线构建。收集来自 S3 层级成功运行的代码输出，并使用正则表达式匹配提取函数定义。随后查询大语言模型（LLM）对这些提取出的函数进行分析，以识别频繁出现的、任务无关的逻辑，将其隔离并提升为可重用技能。虽然目前的实现仅执行单次合成，但该过程本质上是迭代的。随着成功执行案例的积累，智能体可以持续引导、优化或修剪其技能库。此外，根据所需的通用性，研究人员可以调节过滤的宽松程度，以允许更多特定于任务的行为，或保持一个严格的任务无关核心。CaP-Agent0 目前使用的九个合成函数的完整列表见附录 G.1。


3. Parallel Reasoning: Results from tiers S2 and S3 indicate that failures often stem from insufficient test-time exploration rather than a lack of capability. To address this, CaP-Agent0 employs a parallel reasoning strategy inspired by recent ensemble methods (Pan et al., 2025; Jin et al., 2025; Rodionov et al., 2025). At each turn, the system concurrently samples candidate solutions via two configurations: Single-model: 9 queries to one model. Multi-model: 3 queries each to GPT-5.2, Claude Opus 4.5, and Gemini- 3-Pro. To maximize output diversity, we vary sampling temperatures (see Appendix G.2). A central coding agent then synthesizes these candidates into a final code snippet. This parallel approach is applied to both code generation and the decision-making process for multi-turn continuations.
3. 并行推理：来自 S2 和 S3 层级的结果表明，失败往往源于测试时探索不足，而非能力缺失。为解决此问题，CaP-Agent0 采用了受近期集成方法（Pan et al., 2025; Jin et al., 2025; Rodionov et al., 2025）启发的并行推理策略。在每一轮中，系统通过两种配置并发采样候选方案：单模型：对单一模型进行 9 次查询。多模型：分别对 GPT-5.2、Claude Opus 4.5 和 Gemini-3-Pro 进行 3 次查询。为最大化输出多样性，我们改变了采样温度（见附录 G.2）。随后，中央编码智能体将这些候选方案合成为最终的代码片段。这种并行方法同时应用于代码生成和多轮延续的决策过程。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_6.jpg?x=154&y=187&w=1449&h=777&r=0"/>



Figure 7. CaP-Agent0. CaP-Agent0 incorporates an auto-synthesized skill library of auxiliary utility generated by coding agents during CaP-Bench, a visual differencing model (VDM) which provides a textual description of the initial scene and for each subsequent turn what changes have occurred in the scene since, and a parallel reasoning system where multiple coding agents are provided the same prompt. These coding agents then generate candidate code solutions that may solve the task and the ensemble agent must then synthesize these code generations into a final code snippet which is then executed in the Python sandbox containing the robot environment, whether that environment may be a simulator like Robosuite or on a real robot. For more details see Section 4.
图 7. CaP-Agent0。CaP-Agent0 整合了由编码智能体在 CaP-Bench 期间生成的辅助工具自动合成技能库、一个提供初始场景及后续每轮场景变化文本描述的视觉差异模型（VDM），以及一个向多个编码智能体提供相同提示的并行推理系统。这些编码智能体生成可能解决任务的候选代码方案，集成智能体随后将这些代码生成结果合成为最终代码片段，并在包含机器人环境（无论是 Robosuite 等模拟器还是真实机器人）的 Python 沙箱中执行。更多详情请见第 4 节。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_6.jpg?x=177&y=1175&w=659&h=258&r=0"/>



Figure 8. Ablation for CaP-Agent0. (Left): Combining VDM (M4), skill library (+SL), and parallel queries (+1M: only Gemini- 3-Pro, +3M: Gemini-3-Pro, GPT-5.2, and Claude Opus) significantly improves over single-turn setup with low-level API. (Right): On 4 out of 7 CaP-Bench tasks, CaP-Agent0 achieves comparable or better success rates than human expert code in a single-turn setting.
图 8. CaP-Agent0 消融实验。（左）：结合 VDM (M4)、技能库 (+SL) 和并行查询（+1M：仅 Gemini-3-Pro；+3M：Gemini-3-Pro、GPT-5.2 和 Claude Opus）较使用底层 API 的单轮设置有显著提升。（右）：在 7 项 CaP-Bench 任务中的 4 项上，CaP-Agent0 在单轮设置下实现了与人类专家代码相当或更好的成功率。


### 4.1. CaP-Agent0 Performance on CaP-Bench
### 4.1. CaP-Agent0 在 CaP-Bench 上的表现


Evaluated over 100 trials per task, CaP-Agent0 significantly outperforms single-turn baselines by integrating visual differencing, a self-synthesized skill library, and parallel reasoning (Figure 8). Despite operating solely on low-level primitives, the system achieves success rates comparable to or exceeding human-written programs on 4 out of 7 tasks, narrowing the gap toward expert-level performance.
通过整合视觉差异、自合成技能库和并行推理，CaP-Agent0 在每项任务 100 次试验的评估中显著优于单轮基线（图 8）。尽管仅在底层原语上运行，该系统在 7 项任务中的 4 项上实现了与人类编写程序相当或更高的成功率，缩小了与专家级性能的差距。


### 4.2. CaP-Bench++
### 4.2. CaP-Bench++


We further evaluate the performance of CaP-Agent0 on subsets of tasks from LIBERO-PRO and BEHAVIOR. We summarize the results of CaP-Agent0 on 30 manipulation tasks from LIBERO-PRO in Table 2 and compare them against three state-of-the-art VLA methods: OpenVLA (Kim et al., 2024), ${\pi }_{0}$ (Black et al.,2024),and ${\pi }_{0.5}$ (Physical Intelligence et al., 2025). Although these VLA methods are training-based, CaP-Agent0 is a training-free method that has comparable or exceeds the performance of VLA post-training on these tasks. LIBERO-PRO (Zhou et al., 2025) extends the LIBERO (Liu et al., 2023b) benchmark by increasing the perturbations of tasks by reasonable amounts along object attribute perturbations, initial position perturbations, instruction perturbations, and environmental perturbations. CaP-Agent0 and these VLA methods are evaluated along initial position perturbations (Pos) and instruction perturbations (Task). Under Pos perturbations, the initial positions of objects in the scene are swapped with one another (ex: the position of the frypan and moka pot) and under Task perturbations, the instruction is changed so that another object in the scene is manipulated (ex: "Put the moka pot on the stove" → "Put the frypan on the stove").
我们进一步评估了 CaP-Agent0 在 LIBERO-PRO 和 BEHAVIOR 任务子集上的表现。我们在表 2 中总结了 CaP-Agent0 在 30 个 LIBERO-PRO 操作任务上的结果，并将其与三种最先进的 VLA 方法进行了对比：OpenVLA (Kim et al., 2024)、${\pi }_{0}$ (Black et al., 2024) 和 ${\pi }_{0.5}$ (Physical Intelligence et al., 2025)。尽管这些 VLA 方法基于训练，但 CaP-Agent0 是一种无需训练的方法，在这些任务上的表现与经过后训练的 VLA 相当甚至更优。LIBERO-PRO (Zhou et al., 2025) 通过增加对象属性、初始位置、指令和环境等方面的扰动，扩展了 LIBERO (Liu et al., 2023b) 基准测试。CaP-Agent0 和这些 VLA 方法均在初始位置扰动 (Pos) 和指令扰动 (Task) 下进行评估。在 Pos 扰动下，场景中物体的初始位置会相互交换（例如：平底锅和摩卡壶的位置互换）；在 Task 扰动下，指令会发生改变，从而操作场景中的另一个物体（例如：“把摩卡壶放到炉子上” → “把平底锅放到炉子上”）。

Detailed individual task-wise performance can be found in Appendix Section I.

Since VLAs are trained on a different instruction distribution, they perform poorly under task perturbations, whereas CaP-Agent0 remains robust to instruction variations. Furthermore, CaP-Agent0 achieves performance comparable to ${\pi }_{0.5}$ under initial position perturbations.
由于 VLA 是在不同的指令分布上训练的，它们在任务扰动下的表现较差，而 CaP-Agent0 对指令变化保持稳健。此外，在初始位置扰动下，CaP-Agent0 的性能与 ${\pi }_{0.5}$ 相当。


We evaluate our method on two long-horizon mobile manipulation tasks in BEHAVIOR, where an R1Pro wheel-based humanoid is required to pick up a radio from a table and a soda can from the floor. The results over 25 trials for each task are summarized in Table 3, reporting both navigation success rates and task completion success rates. In both tasks, the robot may start with the target object outside its field of view and must actively search for and navigate toward it. Navigation is considered successful if the robot reaches a location within $1\mathrm{\;m}$ of the target.
我们在 BEHAVIOR 的两个长程移动操作任务上评估了我们的方法，要求 R1Pro 轮式人形机器人从桌上拾取收音机，并从地面拾取汽水罐。每个任务 25 次试验的结果汇总于表 3，报告了导航成功率和任务完成成功率。在这两个任务中，机器人可能在起始时目标物体处于视野之外，必须主动搜索并导航至目标。若机器人到达距离目标 $1\mathrm{\;m}$ 以内的位置，则视为导航成功。


The robot can adjust its camera in both horizontal and vertical directions and move both its base and arm to reach the object, resulting in a substantially larger action space than in tabletop manipulation settings. Moreover, potential collisions with surrounding furniture may prevent the robot from reaching the desired pose, leading to partial execution of planned trajectories and increased task complexity.
机器人可以水平和垂直调整摄像头，并移动底座和手臂以触及物体，这导致其动作空间远大于桌面操作环境。此外，与周围家具的潜在碰撞可能阻碍机器人到达目标位姿，导致规划轨迹仅能部分执行，从而增加了任务复杂度。


In the radio pickup task, although the robot often successfully locates and approaches the object, it may lose sight of it or encounter severe occlusions when navigating too closely, due to its limited field of view. This frequently results in missing or poor grasp poses and constitutes a major failure mode for both S3 and the human policy. In contrast, CaP-Agent0 mitigates this issue by repositioning the robot to obtain a better view, achieving substantially higher success rates. For the soda can pickup task, the small object size makes accurate vertical camera alignment critical for localization. S3 often fails by adjusting the camera vertically too early, leading to unsuccessful searches within the time limit. CaP-Agent0 adapts its search strategy based on feedback, improving navigation success. Furthermore, grasping may fail when the can is knocked over, further reducing S3's completion rate. CaP-Agent0 can resample grasp poses after such disturbances and successfully recover, resulting in significantly higher task success and similar performance as human expert.
在收音机拾取任务中，尽管机器人通常能成功定位并接近物体，但由于视野有限，在过于靠近时可能会丢失目标或遇到严重遮挡。这经常导致抓取位姿缺失或不佳，成为 S3 和人类策略的主要失败模式。相比之下，CaP-Agent0 通过重新定位机器人以获得更好的视野来缓解这一问题，实现了显著更高的成功率。对于汽水罐拾取任务，物体尺寸较小，使得精确的垂直摄像头对准对定位至关重要。S3 常因过早进行垂直摄像头调整而失败，导致在限时内搜索无果。CaP-Agent0 根据反馈调整搜索策略，提高了导航成功率。此外，当罐子被撞倒时抓取可能会失败，进一步降低了 S3 的完成率。CaP-Agent0 可以在此类干扰后重新采样抓取位姿并成功恢复，从而显著提高了任务成功率，表现与人类专家相当。


#### 4.3.Let the Agent Experience the Real World
#### 4.3.让智能体体验真实世界


The design of the CaP-Gym environment loop deliberately allows it to directly interface with real-world robot perception and control interfaces, and we additionally demonstrate zero-shot performance of CaP-Agent0 in unseen real-world tasks on real robot embodiments including the Franka Panda and AgiBot G1 without requiring any major cross-embodiment modifications (with the exception of single arm to bimanual control primitive modifications). With no post-training, off-the-shelf VLMs such as Gemini-3-Pro and Claude Opus 4.5 can perform complex long-horizon robotics reasoning and manipulation tasks following natural language instructions. For example, when asked to "find the object under one of the cups" (Figure 12), it mechanically searches through all cups with closed-loop feedback from vision. When the robot is asked to solve a math problem presented in the physical world (Figure 13), it perceives the visual cue, thinks, and selects the correct blocks on the first attempt. We also demonstrate embodied reasoning ability in Figure 15, where CaP-Agent0 exhibits common sense physics reasoning and understands the sensible stacking order for objects of various shapes. Optionally, a human-in-the-loop can also interactively correct the robot's behavior by providing additional feedback in between turns. More details are documented in Appendix A.
CaP-Gym 环境循环的设计特意使其能够直接与真实世界的机器人感知和控制接口对接。此外，我们展示了 CaP-Agent0 在未见过的真实世界任务中的零样本性能，涵盖 Franka Panda 和 AgiBot G1 等真实机器人实体，且无需进行重大的跨实体修改（单臂到双臂控制原语的修改除外）。在无需后训练的情况下，Gemini-3-Pro 和 Claude Opus 4.5 等现成 VLM 能够遵循自然语言指令执行复杂的长程机器人推理和操作任务。例如，当被要求“找到杯子底下的物体”（图 12）时，它会通过视觉闭环反馈机械地搜索所有杯子。当机器人被要求解决物理世界中呈现的数学问题（图 13）时，它能感知视觉线索、进行思考，并在第一次尝试时选择正确的积木。我们还在图 15 中展示了具身推理能力，其中 CaP-Agent0 表现出了常识物理推理，并理解了各种形状物体的合理堆叠顺序。此外，人类可以在循环中通过在轮次间提供额外反馈来交互式地纠正机器人的行为。更多细节记录在附录 A 中。


## 5. CaP-RL
## 5. CaP-RL


CaP-Gym enables on-policy reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) directly on the coding agent. To demonstrate this, we apply Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) (Shao et al., 2024; Guo et al., 2025) to post-train a Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct base model (Hui et al., 2024).
CaP-Gym 实现了直接在编码智能体上进行带可验证奖励的策略强化学习（RLVR）。为证明这一点，我们应用组相对策略优化（GRPO）（Shao et al., 2024; Guo et al., 2025）对 Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct 基础模型（Hui et al., 2024）进行了后训练。


Methodology. We RL post-train on three tasks: Cube Lift, Cube Stack, and Spill Wipe. To ensure stable convergence, we train using the privileged state-based APIs of tier S1. This avoids the noisy reward signals present in tier S2, where compounding perception and control errors can cause otherwise correct programs to fail during execution, introducing credit assignment ambiguity similar to that observed in G1 (Chen et al., 2025).
方法论。我们对三个任务进行了 RL 后训练：立方体提升、立方体堆叠和溢出擦除。为确保稳定收敛，我们使用 S1 层的特权状态 API 进行训练。这避免了 S2 层中存在的噪声奖励信号，在 S2 层中，复合的感知和控制误差可能导致原本正确的程序在执行时失败，从而引入类似于 G1（Chen et al., 2025）中观察到的信用分配模糊性。


Simulation Results. Post-training for 50 iterations per task significantly improves code compilation rates and strategic robustness. When evaluated on S2 (noisy perception), the
仿真结果。每个任务进行 50 次迭代的后训练显著提高了代码编译率和策略稳健性。当在 S2（噪声感知）上进行评估时，


Table 4. Impact of RL Post-Training in Sim and Real. Comparison of success rates between the base model, our RL post-trained agent, and human experts. Simulation results are averaged over 100 trials per task, while real-world deployment on a Franka Emika robot is evaluated over 25 trials.
表 4. RL 后训练在仿真与现实中的影响。基础模型、我们的 RL 后训练智能体与人类专家之间的成功率比较。仿真结果为每个任务 100 次试验的平均值，而 Franka Emika 机器人的真实世界部署则基于 25 次试验进行评估。


<table><tr><td rowspan="2">Method</td><td colspan="3">Simulation (N=100)</td><td colspan="2">Real World (N=25)</td></tr><tr><td>Cube Lift</td><td>Cube Stack</td><td>Spill Wipe</td><td>Cube Lift</td><td>Cube Stack</td></tr><tr><td>Human Expert</td><td>93%</td><td>73%</td><td>100%</td><td>92%</td><td>84%</td></tr><tr><td>Qwen 2.5 Coder 7B</td><td>25%</td><td>4%</td><td>30%</td><td>24%</td><td>12%</td></tr><tr><td>Qwen w/ CaP-RL</td><td>80%</td><td>44%</td><td>93%</td><td>84%</td><td>76%</td></tr></table>
<table><tbody><tr><td rowspan="2">方法</td><td colspan="3">仿真 (N=100)</td><td colspan="2">现实世界 (N=25)</td></tr><tr><td>方块抓取</td><td>方块堆叠</td><td>溢出清理</td><td>方块抓取</td><td>方块堆叠</td></tr><tr><td>人类专家</td><td>93%</td><td>73%</td><td>100%</td><td>92%</td><td>84%</td></tr><tr><td>Qwen 2.5 Coder 7B</td><td>25%</td><td>4%</td><td>30%</td><td>24%</td><td>12%</td></tr><tr><td>Qwen w/ CaP-RL</td><td>80%</td><td>44%</td><td>93%</td><td>84%</td><td>76%</td></tr></tbody></table>


RL post-trained model achieves substantial gains over the base model, as detailed in Table 4.
如表4所示，RL后训练模型相比基础模型取得了显著提升。


Sim-to-Real Transfer. A key advantage of CaP-RL is the minimal Sim-to-Real gap. Because the agent is optimized to reason over abstract perception APIs rather than raw visual features, the learned policy transfers zero-shot to real-world embodiments without having to contend with a visual gap. We validate this on a Franka Emika robot, where the agent retains high success rates for cube lifting (84%) and stacking (76%), demonstrating that improved strategies learned in simulation remain robust under real-world perception noise. Please refer to Appendix Section D for comparing code generation before and after RL post-training.
仿真到现实的迁移。CaP-RL的一个关键优势在于极小的仿真到现实（Sim-to-Real）差距。由于智能体被优化为基于抽象感知API而非原始视觉特征进行推理，所学策略无需处理视觉差异即可零样本迁移至现实世界的实体机器人。我们在Franka Emika机器人上验证了这一点，智能体在立方体抓取（84%）和堆叠（76%）任务中保持了高成功率，证明了在仿真中习得的改进策略在现实世界的感知噪声下依然稳健。关于RL后训练前后的代码生成对比，请参阅附录D节。


## 6. Related Work
## 6. 相关工作


Code as Policies. A growing line of work explores programmatic robot control, where LLMs generate executable code that orchestrates perception and control modules (Gupta & Kembhavi, 2023; Surís et al., 2023; Wei et al., 2022; Yao et al., 2022; Schick et al., 2023; Yang et al., 2024; Yin et al., 2026). In robotics, this paradigm spans grounding LLM plans in physical affordances (Ahn et al., 2022), composing APIs for closed-loop robot behaviors (Singh et al., 2023; Liang et al., 2023; Vemprala et al., 2023), generating Python programs over perception APIs (Huang et al., 2023; Mu et al., 2024; Li et al., 2026; Goldberg et al., 2025), and building embodied reasoning agents (Mu et al., 2023; Zeng et al., 2023; Driess et al., 2023). Structured intermediate representations such as Planning Domain Definition Language (PDDL) and Signal Temporal Logic (STL) (Liu et al., 2023a; Chen et al., 2024b) and persistent state tracking (Yoneda et al., 2024) further improve plan reliability, while executable code has been shown empirically to be a superior agent action representation (Wang et al., 2024a). Recent work scales to multi-robot coordination (Mandi et al., 2024), grounded planning over 3D scene graphs (Rana et al., 2023), and modular vision-language agentic pipelines (Shi et al., 2025; Huang et al., 2022b). Relatedly, Gemini Robotics (Team et al., 2025) highlights hybrid systems integrating tool calling with sensorimotor policies. Across all these settings, agents benefit from iterative self-refinement (Shinn et al., 2023; Madaan et al., 2023; Chen et al., 2024a; Wang et al., 2023c) and from sampling multiple solutions at inference time (Wang et al., 2023b; Li et al., 2022; Yao et al., 2023; Snell et al., 2024); platforms such as OpenHands (Wang et al., 2025) realize this as software engineering agents that write, execute, and debug code in sandboxed environments. Despite this progress, many existing work on agentic coding for robot control typically relies on high-level, human-crafted APIs that encode significant task structure, leaving open the question of how well coding agents perform when operating over low-level primitives closer to how robots are actually programmed by human. CaP-Gym targets this gap by providing an interactive environment that exposes the full primitive stack-down to joint-level perception and control—and CaP-Bench systematically evaluates frontier models across abstraction tiers, enabling principled study of agentic inference-time strategies (multi-turn interaction, execution feedback, visual differencing, ensembled reasoning) as a path toward robotic coding agents.
代码即策略。越来越多的研究探索了程序化机器人控制，即利用大语言模型（LLM）生成可执行代码来编排感知与控制模块（Gupta & Kembhavi, 2023; Surís et al., 2023; Wei et al., 2022; Yao et al., 2022; Schick et al., 2023; Yang et al., 2024; Yin et al., 2026）。在机器人领域，这一范式涵盖了将LLM规划锚定于物理可供性（Ahn et al., 2022）、组合API以实现闭环机器人行为（Singh et al., 2023; Liang et al., 2023; Vemprala et al., 2023）、基于感知API生成Python程序（Huang et al., 2023; Mu et al., 2024; Li et al., 2026; Goldberg et al., 2025）以及构建具身推理智能体（Mu et al., 2023; Zeng et al., 2023; Driess et al., 2023）。规划领域定义语言（PDDL）、信号时序逻辑（STL）（Liu et al., 2023a; Chen et al., 2024b）等结构化中间表示以及持久状态跟踪（Yoneda et al., 2024）进一步提升了规划的可靠性，而经验表明，可执行代码是更优的智能体动作表示（Wang et al., 2024a）。近期研究已扩展至多机器人协作（Mandi et al., 2024）、基于3D场景图的锚定规划（Rana et al., 2023）以及模块化视觉-语言智能体流水线（Shi et al., 2025; Huang et al., 2022b）。相关地，Gemini Robotics（Team et al., 2025）强调了将工具调用与感知运动策略相结合的混合系统。在所有这些场景中，智能体均受益于迭代式自我优化（Shinn et al., 2023; Madaan et al., 2023; Chen et al., 2024a; Wang et al., 2023c）以及推理时的多解采样（Wang et al., 2023b; Li et al., 2022; Yao et al., 2023; Snell et al., 2024）；诸如OpenHands（Wang et al., 2025）等平台将其实现为在沙盒环境中编写、执行和调试代码的软件工程智能体。尽管取得了这些进展，但许多现有的机器人控制智能体编码工作通常依赖于包含大量任务结构的高级人工API，这留下了一个悬而未决的问题：当编码智能体在更接近人类编程机器人方式的底层原语上操作时，其表现如何？CaP-Gym通过提供一个交互式环境填补了这一空白，该环境暴露了完整的原语栈，直至关节级的感知与控制；而CaP-Bench则系统性地评估了不同抽象层级的前沿模型，为研究智能体推理时策略（多轮交互、执行反馈、视觉差异分析、集成推理）提供了原则性路径，旨在推动机器人编码智能体的发展。


Skill Synthesis and RL with LLM-Generated Code. A large body of work uses LLMs as static code generators for reward functions (Ma et al., 2024a; Yu et al., 2023; Xie et al., 2024; Kwon et al., 2023), environment curricula (Liang et al., 2024; Ryu et al., 2025), domain randomization (Ma et al., 2024b), and intrinsic exploration goals (Du et al., 2023), or to synthesize environments and skills autonomously (Wang et al., 2024b; Ahn et al., 2024)—in all cases the LLM is frozen while a separate downstream policy is trained. Complementarily, RL with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for improving the language model itself, with strong results across reasoning (Guo et al., 2025; OpenAI, 2024; Shao et al., 2024), code generation (Le et al., 2022; Shojaee et al., 2023), and interactive agentic settings spanning software engineering (Wei et al., 2025; Pan et al., 2024) and web interaction (Qi et al., 2024). CaP-RL extends RLVR to robot manipulation: rather than using the LLM to produce reward code for a separate policy, we directly fine-tune the language model via GRPO using execution outcomes from physics simulation.
技能合成与基于大模型生成代码的强化学习。大量研究将大模型作为静态代码生成器，用于奖励函数（Ma et al., 2024a; Yu et al., 2023; Xie et al., 2024; Kwon et al., 2023）、环境课程（Liang et al., 2024; Ryu et al., 2025）、域随机化（Ma et al., 2024b）和内在探索目标（Du et al., 2023）的构建，或用于自主合成环境与技能（Wang et al., 2024b; Ahn et al., 2024）——在这些案例中，大模型均保持冻结，同时训练一个独立的下游策略。作为补充，基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为提升语言模型本身的一种强大范式，在推理（Guo et al., 2025; OpenAI, 2024; Shao et al., 2024）、代码生成（Le et al., 2022; Shojaee et al., 2023）以及涵盖软件工程（Wei et al., 2025; Pan et al., 2024）和网页交互（Qi et al., 2024）的交互式智能体场景中均取得了显著成果。CaP-RL 将 RLVR 扩展至机器人操作领域：我们不再使用大模型为独立策略生成奖励代码，而是利用物理模拟的执行结果，通过 GRPO 直接对语言模型进行微调。


Benchmarks for robotics, code generation, and embodied agents. Robotic manipulation benchmarks (Zhu et al., 2020; Liu et al., 2023b; Li et al., 2024a; Mees et al., 2022; James et al., 2019; Li et al., 2024b; Yu et al., 2020; Gu et al., 2023) provide diverse tasks and standardized simulation assets, but typically evaluate fixed policy interfaces rather than executable program synthesis with tiered APIs and multiturn debugging. Software engineering and code generation benchmarks (Chen et al., 2021; Jimenez et al., 2024; Pan et al., 2024; Wang et al., 2025; Li et al., 2022) measure program synthesis in purely digital environments, without embodied perception or physical constraints. Embodied-agent benchmarks (Yang et al., 2025; Chen et al., 2025; Wang et al., 2026; Liu et al., 2024; Shridhar et al., 2020) broaden evaluation to multimodal interactive environments, but do not require agents to generate executable robot-control code under varying abstraction tiers. CaP-Gym targets this intersection: evaluating coding agents on embodied manipulation with verifiable success signals, and explicitly probing how abstraction, multi-turn recovery, and multimodal grounding affect performance.
机器人、代码生成及具身智能体基准测试。机器人操作基准（Zhu et al., 2020; Liu et al., 2023b; Li et al., 2024a; Mees et al., 2022; James et al., 2019; Li et al., 2024b; Yu et al., 2020; Gu et al., 2023）提供了多样的任务和标准化的模拟资源，但通常评估的是固定策略接口，而非具备分层 API 和多轮调试能力的可执行程序合成。软件工程与代码生成基准（Chen et al., 2021; Jimenez et al., 2024; Pan et al., 2024; Wang et al., 2025; Li et al., 2022）在纯数字环境中衡量程序合成，缺乏具身感知或物理约束。具身智能体基准（Yang et al., 2025; Chen et al., 2025; Wang et al., 2026; Liu et al., 2024; Shridhar et al., 2020）将评估范围扩大到多模态交互环境，但并不要求智能体在不同抽象层级下生成可执行的机器人控制代码。CaP-Gym 瞄准了这一交叉领域：在具身操作中评估编码智能体，并利用可验证的成功信号，明确探究抽象、多轮恢复和多模态对齐如何影响性能。


## 7. Future Works and Conclusion
## 7. 未来工作与结论


Programmatic control performs well on long-horizon, reasoning-heavy tasks, but remains brittle for contact-rich behaviors that require tight visual servoing and continuous feedback (e.g., insertion or pouring). One promising direction is hybrid CaP-VLA policies, in which a coding agent manages high-level task logic and recovery while deferring low-level execution to VLA policies. Results from CaP-Bench further highlight several avenues for improving language-model-based agents, including stronger embodiment-aware planning and reasoning, more effective grounding of task-relevant visual information into code generation, improved test-time search, and agent or prompt optimization methods (Khattab et al., 2024). From a robotics perspective, robustness may further improve by incorporating optimization-based control primitives that allow agents to specify task-level constraints and account for collision avoidance during motion planning, rather than relying solely on inverse kinematics solutions that may be suboptimal when directly interpolated to in joint space. Expanding CaP-Gym to additional environments and classical robotics problems (e.g., active and interactive perception) would further stress-test agentic reasoning.
程序化控制在长时程、重推理任务中表现良好，但在需要紧密视觉伺服和连续反馈的接触密集型行为（如插入或倾倒）中仍显脆弱。一个有前景的方向是混合型 CaP-VLA 策略，即由编码智能体管理高层任务逻辑与恢复，同时将底层执行委托给 VLA 策略。CaP-Bench 的结果进一步突显了改进基于语言模型智能体的若干途径，包括更强的具身感知规划与推理、将任务相关视觉信息更有效地对齐至代码生成、改进测试时搜索，以及智能体或提示词优化方法（Khattab et al., 2024）。从机器人技术角度看，通过引入基于优化的控制原语，允许智能体指定任务级约束并在运动规划中考虑避障，而非仅依赖直接插值到关节空间的逆运动学解，鲁棒性有望进一步提升。将 CaP-Gym 扩展至更多环境和经典机器人问题（如主动与交互式感知）将进一步压力测试智能体的推理能力。


We introduce CaP-X, a unified framework for benchmarking and improving coding agents for robot control. CaP-X consists of CaP-Gym, CaP-Bench, CaP-Agent0, and CaP-RL, enabling controlled evaluation across abstraction levels, interaction modes, and learning paradigms. CaP-X frames robot control as a problem of machine intelligence-where agent design, inference-time computation, perception, and control are co-studied—providing a testbed for evaluating and advancing general-purpose embodied intelligence.
我们推出了 CaP-X，这是一个用于基准测试和改进机器人控制编码智能体的统一框架。CaP-X 由 CaP-Gym、CaP-Bench、CaP-Agent0 和 CaP-RL 组成，实现了跨抽象层级、交互模式和学习范式的受控评估。CaP-X 将机器人控制视为一个机器智能问题——即对智能体设计、推理时计算、感知和控制进行协同研究——为评估和推进通用具身智能提供了一个测试平台。


## 8. Impact Statements
## 8. 影响声明


This paper presents work whose goal is to advance the field of machine learning. There are many potential societal consequences of our work, none of which we feel must be specifically highlighted here.
本文旨在推动机器学习领域的发展。我们的工作可能产生许多社会影响，我们认为其中并无需要在此特别强调的内容。

## A. Interactive Real-World Setup
## A. 交互式真实世界设置


In this section, we document the interactive real-world experience with CaP-Agent0 centered around a chat-based web UI, where the user can propose new tasks to the robot, view the step-by-step tool-use results, and offer feedbacks for multi-turn improvement. We will show how this system enables a real-world robot (AgiBot G1) to zero-shot complete novel tasks.
在本节中，我们记录了围绕基于聊天的 Web UI 构建的 CaP-Agent0 交互式真实世界体验。用户可以向机器人提出新任务，查看分步工具使用结果，并提供反馈以进行多轮改进。我们将展示该系统如何使真实世界的机器人（AgiBot G1）能够零样本完成新颖任务。


### A.1. User Interface
### A.1. 用户界面


On the chat UI shown in Figure 9, the user start with choosing task configurations and models. Then they can view the scene description and code generated by the model. As the code is executed on the robot, they also see the step-by-step progress of each tool call, such as the segmentation masks returned by SAM3, Points annotated by Molmo 2, and wrist camera views when the robot arm moves. In between turns, the user can provide additional feedback to the model by typing in the chatbox on the bottom.
在图 9 所示的聊天界面上，用户首先选择任务配置和模型。随后，他们可以查看场景描述和模型生成的代码。当代码在机器人上执行时，他们还能看到每个工具调用的分步进度，例如 SAM3 返回的分割掩码、Molmo 2 标注的点，以及机器人手臂移动时的腕部摄像头视图。在交互轮次之间，用户可以通过底部的聊天框输入额外反馈来引导模型。


The UI also features a 3D visualization powered by Viser (Yi et al., 2025), which shows the live robot URDF, trajectories, and depth pointcloud.
该界面还具备由 Viser (Yi et al., 2025) 支持的 3D 可视化功能，可显示实时机器人 URDF、轨迹和深度点云。


### A.2. Tools
### A.2. 工具


CaP-Agent0, specifically on the AgiBot G1, has access to these APIs for perceiving, reasoning, and interacting.
CaP-Agent0（特别是在 AgiBot G1 上）可以使用以下 API 进行感知、推理和交互。


- get_observation: returns a dictionary of the current head camera image (RGB, depth, and intrinsics), left and right wrist camera images, end-effector 6-DoF force-wrenches, and joint configuration.
- get_observation：返回一个包含当前头部摄像头图像（RGB、深度和内参）、左右腕部摄像头图像、末端执行器 6 自由度力/力矩以及关节配置的字典。


- segment_sam3_text_prompt: given an image and a text prompt, returns a list of segmentation masks and scores.
- segment_sam3_text_prompt：给定图像和文本提示，返回一组分割掩码和分数。


- segment_sam3_point_prompt: given an image and a point coordinate on the image, returns a list of segmentation masks and scores.
- segment_sam3_point_prompt：给定图像和图像上的点坐标，返回一组分割掩码和分数。


- point_prompt_molmo: given an image and a text prompt, returns a list of points on the image pointed out by Molmo 2.
- point_prompt_molmo：给定图像和文本提示，返回由 Molmo 2 指出的图像点列表。


- open_gripper: opens gripper.
- open_gripper：打开夹爪。


- close_gripper: closes gripper.
- close_gripper：关闭夹爪。


- goto_pose: Plans and executes IK to a pose specified by a position and orientation, optionally with a pre-grasp offset and max force-wrench.
- goto_pose：规划并执行逆运动学（IK）以到达由位置和方向指定的位姿，可选择设置预抓取偏移量和最大力矩。


- matrix_to_pose_wxyz_xyz: Converts a $4 \times  4$ transformation matrix to a pose represented in a quaternion and a 3D position.
- matrix_to_pose_wxyz_xyz：将 $4 \times  4$ 变换矩阵转换为由四元数和 3D 位置表示的位姿。


- pose_wxyz_xyz_to_matrix: Converts a pose to a transformation matrix.
- pose_wxyz_xyz_to_matrix：将位姿转换为变换矩阵。


- euler_to_quaternion_wxyz: Converts extrinsic XYZ Euler angles to a quaternion.
- euler_to_quaternion_wxyz：将外在 XYZ 欧拉角转换为四元数。


- quaternion_wxyz_to_euler: Converts quaternion of extrinsic XYZ Euler angles.
- quaternion_wxyz_to_euler：将四元数转换为外在 XYZ 欧拉角。


- query_vlm: Ask a question with text and images to an expert VLM model (Gemini-3-Pro)
- query_vlm：向专家 VLM 模型（Gemini-3-Pro）提出包含文本和图像的问题。


- go_forward: Move forward 1 meter.
- go_forward：向前移动 1 米。


- turn_left_45_degrees: Turn left 45 degrees.
- turn_left_45_degrees：向左转 45 度。


- turn_right_45_degrees: Turn right 45 degrees.
- turn_right_45_degrees：向右转 45 度。


- goto_planar_position: Plan and execute IK to a position with planar motion constraint, but no orientation (yaw) requirement.
- goto_planar_position：规划并执行逆运动学（IK）以到达具有平面运动约束的位置，无需考虑方向（偏航角）。


- convert_depth_to_pointcloud: Given a depth image, intrinsics, and extrinsics, convert the depth image into a pointcloud.
- convert_depth_to_pointcloud：给定深度图像、内参和外参，将深度图像转换为点云。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_19.jpg?x=159&y=343&w=1434&h=1534&r=0"/>



Figure 9. An example of the web UI, where users can select the task and model at the top, view the model's responses and execution details in the middle, and provide instructions at the bottom.
图 9. Web UI 示例，用户可在顶部选择任务和模型，在中间查看模型的响应和执行详情，并在底部提供指令。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_20.jpg?x=294&y=598&w=1171&h=1051&r=0"/>



Figure 10. Viser (Yi et al., 2025) visualization section of the web UI.
图 10. Web UI 中的 Viser (Yi et al., 2025) 可视化部分。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_21.jpg?x=220&y=197&w=1318&h=711&r=0"/>



Figure 11. An example of CaP-Agent0 locating and grasping an auto pencil refill holder, where it uses Molmo2 to locate the object.
图 11. CaP-Agent0 定位并抓取自动铅笔芯盒的示例，它使用 Molmo2 来定位物体。


- forward_kinematics: Given a robot configuration, compute the end-effector pose.
- forward_kinematics：给定机器人配置，计算末端执行器的位姿。


- overlay_eef_axis_on_image: Visualize end-effector pose on a camera image by rendering the 3D axis on top.
- overlay_eef_axis_on_image：通过在相机图像上叠加渲染 3D 轴，实现末端执行器位姿的可视化。


- overlay_segmentation_masks: Visualize segmentation masks on an image.
- overlay_segmentation_masks：在图像上可视化分割掩码。


- say_something: Convey some intent to the user.
- say_something：向用户传达某种意图。


Among the tools, the 3D rigid body transformation helpers are provided although technically not strictly necessary. We find that when not provided, these functions are almost always written by the models who make mistakes from time to time.
在这些工具中，虽然 3D 刚体变换辅助函数在技术上并非绝对必要，但我们提供了它们。我们发现，如果不提供这些函数，模型几乎总是会自行编写，且偶尔会出错。


Visualization tools such as overlay_eef_axis_on_image and overlay_segmentation_masks enables advanced multi-modal reasoning when the output images are passed to an expert VLM via query_vlm. This allows, for example, code execution conditioning based on if the expert VLM answered "which of these segmentation masks should I pick?".
诸如 overlay_eef_axis_on_image 和 overlay_segmentation_masks 之类的可视化工具，在将输出图像通过 query_vlm 传递给专家 VLM 时，能够实现高级的多模态推理。例如，这允许基于专家 VLM 对“我应该选择这些分割掩码中的哪一个？”的回答来进行代码执行条件判断。


### A.3. Real World Tasks
### A.3. 真实世界任务


In this section, we show visualizations of CaP-Agent0 completing tasks in the real world. All experiments are zero-shot. The agent's execution details are condensed and presented as pseudo sub-steps, while CaP-Agent0 writes the underlying code in greater detail using tools available in A.2. Raw code example is available in Appendix E.
在本节中，我们展示了 CaP-Agent0 在真实世界中完成任务的可视化过程。所有实验均为零样本（zero-shot）。智能体的执行细节被浓缩并呈现为伪子步骤，而 CaP-Agent0 则使用 A.2 节中提供的工具编写更详细的底层代码。原始代码示例可在附录 E 中找到。


#### A.3.1. NEEDLE IN A HAYSTACK
#### A.3.1. 大海捞针


In this task, we evaluate the ability of CaP-Agent0 to find "needles in a haystack." Specifically, in a cluttered scene containing diverse objects, the robot is tasked with locating and grasping an auto pencil refill holder, a relatively uncommon item. Such uncommon objects are often challenging for end-to-end learning policies such as VLAs. In contrast, CaP-Agent0 leverages pretrained VLMs to successfully localize and retrieve the target object, as shown in Figure 11.
在此任务中，我们评估 CaP-Agent0“大海捞针”的能力。具体而言，在包含多种物体的杂乱场景中，机器人需要定位并抓取一个相对罕见的物品——自动铅笔芯盒。此类罕见物体对于 VLA 等端到端学习策略来说通常具有挑战性。相比之下，如图 11 所示，CaP-Agent0 利用预训练的 VLM 成功定位并取回了目标物体。


#### A.3.2. MECHANICAL SEARCH
#### A.3.2. 机械搜索


In this task, three inverted cups are placed on a table, and the robot is instructed to retrieve a green lime hidden beneath one of them. This occluded object retrieval problem is commonly referred to as mechanical search (Huang et al., 2022a). Because the lime is concealed by the cups, the robot must systematically explore each cup to locate it. A representative planning and execution example is shown in Figure 12.
在此任务中，桌上放置了三个倒扣的杯子，机器人需取回隐藏在其中一个杯子下的青柠。这种遮挡物体的检索问题通常被称为机械搜索（Huang et al., 2022a）。由于青柠被杯子遮挡，机器人必须系统地探索每个杯子以找到它。图 12 展示了一个典型的规划与执行示例。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_22.jpg?x=288&y=189&w=1180&h=1557&r=0"/>



Figure 12. Mechanical search planning and execution example. The left column shows the agent planning process and the right column shows the physical robot execution.
图 12. 机械搜索的规划与执行示例。左列显示智能体的规划过程，右列显示物理机器人的执行过程。


#### A.3.3. MULTIMODAL SYMBOLIC REASONING
#### A.3.3. 多模态符号推理


In this task, we evaluate the multimodal symbolic reasoning capabilities of CaP-Agent0 by requiring it to solve a mathematical equation formed by numbered wooden blocks. The robot must first perceive the scene to interpret the equation and then grasp the correct block and place it in correct location to complete the solution, as shown in Figure 13.
在此任务中，我们通过要求 CaP-Agent0 求解由带数字的木块组成的数学等式，来评估其多模态符号推理能力。如图 13 所示，机器人必须首先感知场景以解读等式，然后抓取正确的木块并将其放置在正确位置以完成求解。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_23.jpg?x=214&y=245&w=1328&h=1756&r=0"/>



Figure 13. Example of a Multimodal Symbolic Reasoning task, where the robot is asked to solve the problem of 59 plus 8.
图 13. 多模态符号推理任务示例，机器人被要求解决 59 加 8 的问题。


#### A.3.4. LEARNING FROM HUMAN FEEDBACK
#### A.3.4. 从人类反馈中学习


CaP-Agent0 is able to incorporate human feedback and adjust its code generation accordingly to complete the task. As shown in Figure 14, the robot is instructed to pick up an apple but fails in the initial attempt due to an excessively high grasp pose. After receiving the feedback "grasped the apple too high," CaP-Agent0 modifies the generated code and successfully completes the task on the second attempt.
CaP-Agent0 能够整合人类反馈并相应地调整其代码生成以完成任务。如图 14 所示，机器人被指示拿起一个苹果，但由于抓取姿态过高，首次尝试失败。在收到“抓取苹果的位置太高”的反馈后，CaP-Agent0 修改了生成的代码，并在第二次尝试中成功完成了任务。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_24.jpg?x=252&y=442&w=1248&h=1335&r=0"/>



Figure 14. Example of picking up an apple. While the first attempt fails, CaP-Agent0 takes human feedback as input, adjusts the code and completes the task successfully.
图 14. 拿起苹果的示例。虽然第一次尝试失败，但 CaP-Agent0 将人类反馈作为输入，调整代码并成功完成了任务。


#### A.3.5. EMBODIED REASONING
#### A.3.5. 具身推理


This task evaluates the embodied reasoning ability of CaP-Agent0, where the robot is asked to "stack objects as high as possible". Because the scene contains both square and round objects, the robot must reason about their physical properties to determine a stable stacking strategy. As shown in Figure 15, CaP-Agent0 learns to place round objects on top of square ones to maximize stability.
此任务评估 CaP-Agent0 的具身推理能力，要求机器人“尽可能高地堆叠物体”。由于场景中同时包含方形和圆形物体，机器人必须推理它们的物理属性以确定稳定的堆叠策略。如图 15 所示，CaP-Agent0 学会了将圆形物体放置在方形物体之上，以实现稳定性最大化。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_25.jpg?x=215&y=238&w=1323&h=1760&r=0"/>



Figure 15. Example of CaP-Agent0 stacking round objects on top of square objects to form the tallest possible stable stack.
图 15. CaP-Agent0 将圆形物体堆叠在方形物体之上以形成最高稳定堆叠的示例。


#### A.3.6. TOOL GENERALIZATION WITH DOMAIN KNOWLEDGE
#### A.3.6. 结合领域知识的工具泛化


This task demonstrates the versatility of the code-as-policy interface, where CaP-Agent0 can use tools from arbituary Python packages to assist with the task. We ask the robot to "take the elevator downstairs", which suggests locating and pressing the button, and moving into the elevator. Since the robot is positioned at an angle with respect to the wall, it is not immediately obvious in which direction the button should be pushed. CaP-Agent0 is able to invoke SciPy RANSAC algorithm on the segmented wall pointcloud, and compute the surface normal direction, shown in Figure 16.
此任务展示了“代码即策略”（code-as-policy）接口的多功能性，CaP-Agent0 可调用任意 Python 包中的工具来辅助完成任务。我们要求机器人“乘电梯下楼”，这需要定位并按下按钮，然后进入电梯。由于机器人相对于墙壁呈一定角度，按下按钮的方向并不直观。CaP-Agent0 能够对分割后的墙壁点云调用 SciPy RANSAC 算法，并计算出表面法线方向，如图 16 所示。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_26.jpg?x=292&y=461&w=1175&h=1557&r=0"/>



Figure 16. Example of robot pushing the elevator button.
图 16. 机器人按下电梯按钮的示例。

## B. 完整基准测试表


We present the full results from CaP-Bench in Figure 17. From top to bottom are code compilation success rate, average dense reward, and average task success rate.
我们在图 17 中展示了 CaP-Bench 的完整结果。从上到下依次为代码编译成功率、平均密集奖励和平均任务成功率。

Therefore, we only evaluatd all models for the multi-turn setup.
图 17. CaP-Bench 完整结果。从上到下依次为代码编译成功率、平均任务奖励和平均任务成功率。注意，对于 Re-Stack 任务，在简单的任务提示且无视觉输入的情况下，我们未观察到模型会先编写代码检查初始条件再执行任务，从而导致失败。因此，我们仅针对多轮设置评估了所有模型。


## C. Additional Takeaways
## C. 额外收获


In-Context Examples of API Usage improves performance. In the docstring of each API used in S4, we provided a brief description of the API, the expected datatype, and shape for each input and output. However, due to low code compilation successes from open source models in the initial experiments, we hypothesize that additional prompting may be necessary to increase model performance. Therefore, in addition to the components above, we added API usage examples in the docstring.
上下文中的 API 使用示例可提升性能。在 S4 中使用的每个 API 的文档字符串（docstring）中，我们提供了 API 的简要说明以及每个输入和输出的预期数据类型和形状。然而，由于开源模型在初步实验中的代码编译成功率较低，我们推测可能需要额外的提示来提高模型性能。因此，除上述组件外，我们在文档字符串中增加了 API 使用示例。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_28.jpg?x=156&y=461&w=1444&h=546&r=0"/>



Figure 18. Per-model breakdown of usefulness of in-context API Usage
图 18. 上下文中 API 使用示例对各模型的有效性分析


We present the results in Figure 3 and Figure 4, and a per-model breakdown in Figure 18. We observe that almost all models benefited from adding additional context of examples of how to use the low-level APIs.
我们在图 3 和图 4 中展示了结果，并在图 18 中提供了各模型的详细分析。我们观察到，几乎所有模型都受益于添加了如何使用底层 API 的额外上下文示例。


## D. Qualitative Analysis of CaP-RL Post-Training Effects
## D. CaP-RL 训练后效果的定性分析


In this section, we analyze the qualitative behavioral shifts induced by on-policy reinforcement learning (GRPO) on the Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct base model. We focus on the Stack Red Cube on Green Cube task to illustrate how RL mitigates fundamental instruction-following failures and induces robust geometric reasoning. Methodologically, CaP-RL leverages the privileged S1 tier to stabilize training by removing perception noise. Below we show the code block examples before and after CaP-RL Post-Training.
在本节中，我们分析了策略内强化学习（GRPO）对 Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct 基础模型所引发的定性行为转变。我们重点关注“将红方块堆叠在绿方块上”的任务，以说明强化学习如何缓解基本的指令遵循失败并诱导稳健的几何推理。在方法论上，CaP-RL 利用特权 S1 层通过消除感知噪声来稳定训练。下面我们展示了 CaP-RL 训练前后的代码块示例。


Before CaP-RL Post-Training Model Behavior. Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct base model code generation example on the task Stack Red Cube on Green Cube prior to on-policy reinforcement learning with CaP-RL:
CaP-RL 训练前的模型行为。Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct 基础模型在进行 CaP-RL 策略内强化学习前，针对“将红方块堆叠在绿方块上”任务的代码生成示例：


---



import numpy as np
import numpy as np


#Get the pose of the green cube
#获取绿方块的位姿


green_cube_position, green_cube_quaternion_wxyz, _ = get_object_pose("green cube")
green_cube_position, green_cube_quaternion_wxyz, _ = get_object_pose("green cube")


#Get the pose of the red cube
#获取红方块的位姿


red_cube_position, red_cube_quaternion_wxyz, _ = get_object_pose("red cube")
red_cube_position, red_cube_quaternion_wxyz, _ = get_object_pose("red cube")


#Calculate the placement position for the red cube
#计算红色方块的放置位置


placement_position = np.array(green_cube_position) + np.array([0, 0, 0.05]) # 5 cm
placement_position = np.array(green_cube_position) + np.array([0, 0, 0.05]) # 5 厘米


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;above the green cube
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;在绿色方块上方


#Move the robot to the placement position
#将机器人移动到放置位置


goto_pose(placement_position, (0, 0, 1, 0)), z_approach=0.1) # Use a slight z_approach
goto_pose(placement_position, (0, 0, 1, 0)), z_approach=0.1) # 使用微小的 z_approach


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for precision
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;以确保精度


#Open the gripper to release the red cube
#打开夹爪以释放红色方块


open_gripper()
open_gripper()
