After CaP-RL Post-Training Model Behavior. Code generation example of Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct model after on-policy reinforcement learning with CaP-RL on the task Stack Red Cube on Green Cube :
CaP-RL 后训练模型行为。Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct 模型在通过 CaP-RL 进行策略内强化学习后，针对“将红色方块堆叠在绿色方块上”任务的代码生成示例：


---



import numpy as np
import numpy as np


#Get the positions and extents of the red and green cubes
#获取红色和绿色方块的位置及范围


red_cube_pos, _, red_cube_extent = get_object_pose("red cube", return_bbox_extent=True)
red_cube_pos, _, red_cube_extent = get_object_pose("red cube", return_bbox_extent=True)


green_cube_pos, _, green_cube_extent = get_object_pose("green cube", return_bbox_extent
green_cube_pos, _, green_cube_extent = get_object_pose("green cube", return_bbox_extent


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;=True)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;=True)


#Calculate the placement position on top of the green cube
#计算绿色方块顶部的放置位置


placement_pos = green_cube_pos + np.array([0, 0, red_cube_extent[2] / 2 +
placement_pos = green_cube_pos + np.array([0, 0, red_cube_extent[2] / 2 +


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;green_cube_extent[2] / 2])
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;green_cube_extent[2] / 2])


#Sample a grasp pose for the red cube
#为红色方块采样抓取位姿


grasp_pos, grasp_quat = sample_grasp_pose("red cube")
grasp_pos, grasp_quat = sample_grasp_pose("red cube")


#Move to the grasp pose and approach
#移动至抓取位姿并靠近


goto_pose(grasp_pos, grasp_quat, z_approach=0.1)
goto_pose(grasp_pos, grasp_quat, z_approach=0.1)


#Close the gripper to grasp the red cube
#闭合夹爪以抓取红色方块


close_gripper()
close_gripper()


#Move to the placement position
#移动至放置位置


goto_pose(placement_pos, (0, 0, 1, 0)), z_approach=0.1)
goto_pose(placement_pos, (0, 0, 1, 0)), z_approach=0.1)


#Open the gripper to release the red cube
#打开夹爪以释放红色方块


open_gripper()
open_gripper()


---



Pre-RL Failure Modes: Step Skipping and Hallucinated State. Prior to RL post-training, the base model frequently exhibits "step skipping", a failure mode where the agent attempts to satisfy the final goal state without executing the necessary prerequisites. As shown in the pre-RL snippet, the model correctly identifies the target location (placement_position) but fails to grasp the red cube. It attempts to move the gripper directly to the placement target and open it, seemingly hallucinating that it is already holding the object.
RL前失败模式：步骤跳过与状态幻觉。在RL后训练之前，基础模型常表现出“步骤跳过”，即智能体在未执行必要前提条件的情况下试图直接达成最终目标状态。如RL前代码片段所示，模型虽能正确识别目标位置（placement_position），却未能抓取红色方块。它试图直接将夹爪移至放置目标并打开，仿佛产生了已抓取物体的幻觉。


Post-RL Improvement: Causal Sequencing and Geometric Generalization. After GRPO training, two critical improvements emerge:
RL后改进：因果序列与几何泛化。经过GRPO训练后，出现了两项关键改进：


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_30.jpg?x=158&y=195&w=1438&h=614&r=0"/>



Figure 19. CaP-RL Finetuned Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct deployed on the real task put the red cube on the green cube. Human Oracle code gets 21/25 task successes in real. Prior to reinforcement learning, we see behaviors such as grasp approaches on the green cube as the first action, rather than a more sensible approach on the red cube first.
图19。部署于真实任务“将红色方块放置在绿色方块上”的CaP-RL微调版Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct。人类专家代码在真实环境中取得21/25的任务成功率。在强化学习之前，我们观察到诸如将“靠近绿色方块”作为首个动作的行为，而非更合理的“先靠近红色方块”。


1. Causal Sequencing: The model correctly synthesizes the full manipulation chain: Identify $\rightarrow$ Grasp $\rightarrow$ Transport $\rightarrow$ Release. It learns through environment interaction and reward feedback signals that the causal dependency that an object must be grasped (via close_gripper) before it can be placed.
1. 因果序列：模型正确合成了完整的操作链：识别 $\rightarrow$ 抓取 $\rightarrow$ 搬运 $\rightarrow$ 释放。它通过环境交互和奖励反馈信号学习到因果依赖关系，即物体必须先被抓取（通过close_gripper）才能被放置。


2. Dynamic Geometric Reasoning: Instead of using hard-coded offsets, the RL-trained model utilizes the return_bbox_extent = True parameter to dynamically calculate the stacking height based on object dimensions (red_extent[2]/2 + green_extent[2]/2). This indicates a shift from memorization to grounded geometric reasoning.
2. 动态几何推理：RL 训练模型不再使用硬编码偏移量，而是利用 return_bbox_extent = True 参数，根据物体尺寸（red_extent[2]/2 + green_extent[2]/2）动态计算堆叠高度。这表明模型已从死记硬背转向基于实体的几何推理。


Zero-shot Generalization to Non-privileged Physical World Setups. Although the model is only post-trained on the privileged S1 tier, the resulting policies demonstrate robust zero-shot transfer to the non-privileged S2 tier. Consequently, the model functions effectively in physical real-world setups, as shown in Figure 19.
对非特权物理世界设置的零样本泛化。尽管模型仅在特权 S1 层级上进行了后训练，但所得策略在非特权 S2 层级上展现出了稳健的零样本迁移能力。因此，如图 19 所示，该模型在物理现实世界设置中也能有效运行。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_30.jpg?x=156&y=1369&w=1441&h=392&r=0"/>



Figure 20. CaP-RL Finetuned Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct successfully deployed on similar task variants. Demonstrates that base model is still capable of instruction following.
图 20. 经 CaP-RL 微调的 Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct 成功部署于相似任务变体。证明了基础模型仍具备指令遵循能力。


Zero-Shot Generalization to Task Variants. We observe instruction-following and zero-shot generalization to similar task variants after RL post-training, as seen in 20. The same policy successfully executes variants such as "put the tennis ball on the green cube" or tasks involving randomized object colors, as the underlying logic relies on abstract properties (bounding boxes) rather than overfitting to specific entity names or training instance scales.
对任务变体的零样本泛化。正如 20 所见，在 RL 后训练后，我们观察到了指令遵循和对相似任务变体的零样本泛化能力。同一策略可成功执行诸如“将网球放在绿色方块上”或涉及随机物体颜色的任务，因为其底层逻辑依赖于抽象属性（边界框），而非过拟合于特定的实体名称或训练实例规模。


## E. CaP-Agent0 Case Studies
## E. CaP-Agent0 案例研究


### E.1. Real-World Case Studies
### E.1. 现实世界案例研究


E.1.1. COMMON SENSE PHYSICS-AWARE TASK DECOMPOSITION
E.1.1. 基于常识物理的复杂任务分解


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_31.jpg?x=155&y=365&w=1448&h=292&r=0"/>



Figure 21. "Stack these as high as you can."
图 21. “尽可能高地堆叠这些物体。”


We validate CaP-Agent0 on a real-world Franka Panda platform using a set of geometrically heterogeneous objects: a yellow cube, a blue cube, and a tennis ball. The agent was given the open-ended instruction: "stack these as high as you can." with no additional prompt context outside of API usage documentation and the multimodal agent initial scene description.
我们在 Franka Panda 现实世界平台上验证了 CaP-Agent0，使用了一组几何形状各异的物体：一个黄色方块、一个蓝色方块和一个网球。代理收到的开放式指令为：“尽可能高地堆叠这些物体。”除 API 使用文档和多模态代理初始场景描述外，未提供任何额外的提示上下文。


Crucially, the task prompt provides neither a specific stacking sequence nor any semantic description of the scene or its objects. While a standard visuomotor policy might attempt to stack objects in detection order, potentially attempting to balance a cube on top of the spherical ball, CaP-Agent0 demonstrated common-sense embodied physical reasoning by deriving the only stable construction order.
关键在于，任务提示既未提供具体的堆叠顺序，也未提供场景或物体的任何语义描述。虽然标准的视觉运动策略可能会尝试按检测顺序堆叠物体，甚至可能尝试将方块平衡在球体上方，但 CaP-Agent0 通过推导出唯一稳定的构建顺序，展现了基于常识的具身物理推理能力。


This behavior is enabled by the CaP-Agent0 auxiliary VDM multimodal agent that extracts task-relevant image information before code generation begins. Prompted to "describe the initial state of the environment with the goal of the task in mind," the VLM emits the following context for the coding agent's initial turn:
这种行为得益于 CaP-Agent0 的辅助 VDM 多模态代理，它在代码生成开始前提取了与任务相关的图像信息。在被提示“结合任务目标描述环境的初始状态”时，VLM 为编码代理的初始轮次输出了以下上下文：


"...The cubes appear to have flat surfaces suitable for stacking, while the tennis ball is spherical and would likely need to be placed on top or handled carefully."
“……方块表面平坦，适合堆叠，而网球呈球形，可能需要放置在最上方或小心处理。”


Leveraging this textual grounding, the coding agent explicitly decomposed the problem based on stability constraints. The full code generated by the CaP-Agent0 agent for completing this task is found in Appendix H.1.
利用这种文本基础，编码代理明确地基于稳定性约束分解了问题。CaP-Agent0 完成此任务生成的完整代码见附录 H.1。


E.1.2. IMPLICIT MULTI-STEP REASONING FOR OBSTRUCTED GOALS
E.1.2. 针对受阻目标的隐式多步推理


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_31.jpg?x=156&y=1451&w=1447&h=292&r=0"/>



Figure 22. "Place the blue cube on top of the yellow cube."
图 22. “将蓝色方块放在黄色方块上方。”


We evaluate CaP-Agent0 on a task where the Franka Panda must place a blue cube on top of a yellow cube. In the initial state, the cubes form a three-object tower: blue is at the base, supporting yellow, which in turn supports a green cube (Figure 22).
我们评估了 CaP-Agent0 在 Franka Panda 必须将蓝色方块放置在黄色方块之上的任务中的表现。在初始状态下，这些方块构成了一个三层塔：蓝色方块位于底部，支撑着黄色方块，黄色方块上方又支撑着一个绿色方块（图 22）。


The goal prompt "place the blue cube on top of the yellow cube" is linguistically underspecified; it contains no mention of the green obstruction nor the fact that the blue target currently supports the yellow destination.
提示词“将蓝色方块放置在黄色方块上方”在语言上描述不足；它既未提及绿色障碍物，也未说明蓝色目标方块当前正支撑着黄色目标方块这一事实。


CaP-Agent0 resolves this dependency through its auxiliary multimodal perception layer. Before code generation, the VLM provides the coding agent with a high-level strategic prior:
CaP-Agent0 通过其辅助多模态感知层解决了这一依赖问题。在生成代码之前，VLM 为编码智能体提供了高层级的策略先验：


"...the blue cube is at the bottom of the stack, underneath the yellow cube, and the yellow cube is underneath a green cube. This implies a complex manipulation task where the robot will likely need to: 1. Remove the top (green) cube. 2. Remove the middle (yellow) cube to access the blue one, or move the stack. 3. Ultimately re-arrange them such that the blue cube ends up on top of the yellow one. The straightforward description is that the target blue cube is currently obstructed and supporting the target destination object (the yellow cube)."
“……蓝色方块位于堆叠的最底部，在黄色方块下方，而黄色方块又位于绿色方块下方。这意味着一项复杂的操纵任务，机器人很可能需要：1. 移除顶部的（绿色）方块。2. 移除中间的（黄色）方块以接触蓝色方块，或者移动整个堆叠。3. 最终重新排列它们，使得蓝色方块位于黄色方块之上。直观的描述是，目标蓝色方块目前被遮挡，且支撑着目标目的地物体（黄色方块）。”


This behavior demonstrates that programmatic agents, when augmented with a dedicated perception-to-text grounding layer, can derive complex manipulation strategies traditionally requiring extensive task-specific imitation learning data or manual state-machine design. The full executable rollout is provided in Appendix H.2.
这种行为表明，当程序化智能体配备了专门的感知到文本的接地层（grounding layer）时，能够推导出复杂的操纵策略，而这些策略传统上需要大量的特定任务模仿学习数据或手动设计状态机。完整的可执行过程见附录 H.2。


### E.2. Simulation Case Studies
### E.2. 仿真案例研究


#### E.2.1. VERIFICATION AND RETRY BEHAVIOR ENABLED BY MULTITURN DESIGN
#### E.2.1. 多轮设计实现的验证与重试行为


This case study comes from the "pick up the red cube" task from Robosuite ported into CaP-Gym. Unlike one-shot code generation frameworks, the multi-turn architecture of CaP-Agent0 allows for emergent agentic resilience. In several simulation trials, we observed instances where a planned grasp was physically executed but failed to successfully lift the object due to physics-engine stochasticity or sub-optimal contact points. Rather than terminating the task upon failure, the agent utilized the subsequent turn's observation to verify that the goal condition (e.g., ${z}_{\text{ object }} > {z}_{\text{ table }}$ ) remained unfulfilled. As shown in the generated logic, the agent autonomously synthesized a recovery routine branch. This capacity to reason about execution failures and reset the environment state demonstrates that CaP-Agent0 can function as a closed-loop reactive agent rather than a static script generator.
本案例研究源自 Robosuite 中移植到 CaP-Gym 的“拾取红色方块”任务。与一次性代码生成框架不同，CaP-Agent0 的多轮架构实现了涌现式的智能体韧性。在多次仿真试验中，我们观察到一些实例：规划的抓取动作虽已物理执行，但由于物理引擎的随机性或接触点不理想，未能成功提起物体。智能体并未在失败时终止任务，而是利用后续轮次的观测来验证目标条件（例如 ${z}_{\text{ object }} > {z}_{\text{ table }}$ ）是否仍未满足。如生成的逻辑所示，智能体自主合成了恢复例程分支。这种针对执行失败进行推理并重置环境状态的能力，证明了 CaP-Agent0 可以作为闭环反应式智能体运行，而非仅仅是一个静态脚本生成器。


---



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;...



masks = segment_sam3_text_prompt(rgb, "red cube")

#### E.2.2. PERCEPTION MODULE CASCADE FAILURE FALLBACKS
#### E.2.2. 感知模块级联故障的回退机制


This case study comes from the "wipe up the brown spill" task from Robosuite ported into CaP-Gym. The model frequently constructs robust perception pipelines that utilize hierarchical fallbacks. It understands that a generic text prompt might fail or be imprecise. In several trials, the model employs a VLM (Molmo) to visually ground the target ("brown spill") into a specific 2D point, and then uses that point to prompt a segmentation model (SAM3) for a precise mask. If this high-precision
本案例研究源自 Robosuite 中移植到 CaP-Gym 的“擦除棕色污渍”任务。模型经常构建出利用分层回退机制的稳健感知流水线。它理解通用的文本提示可能会失败或不够精确。在多次试验中，模型采用 VLM (Molmo) 将目标（“棕色污渍”）在视觉上定位为特定的二维点，然后利用该点提示分割模型 (SAM3) 获取精确掩码。如果这种高精度


method fails, it falls back to broader text prompts like "stain" or "brown object".
方法失败，它会回退到更宽泛的文本提示，如“污渍”或“棕色物体”。

#### E.2.3. Geometric Reasoning for Grasp Selection
#### E.2.3. 抓取选择的几何推理


This case study illustrates how CaP-Agent0 enhances sub-symbolic planners by injecting context-aware strategy. While modules like Contact-GraspNet infer many 6D grasp poses along with confidence scores, the learned scoring lacks awareness of the broader task setting. For this tabletop scenario, the agent correctly identified that a top-down approach strategy is inherently more reliable than side-approaches, regardless of their raw grasp scores.
本案例研究展示了 CaP-Agent0 如何通过注入情境感知策略来增强次符号规划器。虽然 Contact-GraspNet 等模块能推断出许多带有置信度分数的 6D 抓取姿态，但学习到的评分缺乏对更广泛任务环境的感知。对于此桌面场景，智能体正确识别出，无论原始抓取分数如何，自上而下的接近策略本质上都比侧向接近更可靠。


To enforce this strategy, the agent autonomously synthesized a geometric constraint wrapper. By computing the alignment between grasp approach vectors and the world vertical, the generated code filtered out high-scoring but suboptimal side-grasps, explicitly selecting a vertical candidate to maximize stability. The agent also synthesized an autonomous fallback branch: if this strict strategy yielded no candidates, the logic reverted to the global maximum score to prevent execution stagnation. This demonstrates the agent's capacity to wrap generic tools in context-specific logic, bridging the gap between raw geometric perception and high-level task semantics.
为了执行该策略，智能体自主合成了一个几何约束包装器。通过计算抓取接近向量与世界垂直方向的对齐度，生成的代码过滤掉了分数虽高但次优的侧向抓取，明确选择了垂直候选方案以最大化稳定性。智能体还合成了一个自主回退分支：如果这一严格策略未产生候选方案，逻辑将恢复为全局最高分，以防止执行停滞。这证明了智能体能够将通用工具封装在特定情境的逻辑中，弥合了原始几何感知与高层任务语义之间的鸿沟。


Crucially, the automatically synthesized skill library (Appendix G.1) contains an analogous grasp filter, serving as a primary example of the agent's capacity to synthesize task-agnostic geometric logic into its persistent codebase.
至关重要的是，自动合成的技能库（附录 G.1）包含一个类似的抓取过滤器，这是智能体将其任务无关的几何逻辑合成到其持久代码库中能力的典型范例。


---



...

print ("正在规划抓取...")

if len(grasp_poses) == 0:

#### E.2.4. 代码生成集成提升鲁棒性


In this case study, we analyze the differences in code generation for a VDM agent which uses a single query vs a model ensemble. All generated code is for the cube restack task. The following is a portion of the initial generation from single query.
在本案例研究中，我们分析了 VDM 智能体在使用单次查询与模型集成时，代码生成方面的差异。所有生成的代码均针对立方体堆叠任务。以下是单次查询初始生成代码的一部分。

...



---



Notice how there is no fallback for the sample_grasp_pose () generation. When the initial code was executed, the outputted grasp was invalid. The model reasoned that the grasp was invalid because it was too close to the origin, so in the subsequent generation, the model retroactively implemented a fallback which only prevents the failure case it just encountered.
请注意，sample_grasp_pose () 的生成过程缺乏回退机制。当初始代码执行时，输出的抓取点无效。模型推断该抓取点无效是因为其过于靠近原点，因此在后续生成中，模型追溯性地实现了一个仅能防止其刚遇到的故障情况的回退方案。

## F. Low-Level Perception and Control Primitives
## F. 底层感知与控制原语


This section provides the complete specifications for the low-level perception and control primitives used in CaP-Bench, including function signatures, interface definitions, and documentation strings. These primitives constitute the exact specifications provided to agents in Tier S3. Tier S4 utilizes an identical primitive set, but with in-context usage examples (the Example: sections within docstrings) stripped. Tiers S1 and S2 operate on high-level abstractions that are constructed by composing these fundamental primitives.
本节提供了CaP-Bench所用底层感知与控制原语的完整规范，包括函数签名、接口定义及文档字符串。这些原语构成了提供给S3层智能体的确切规范。S4层使用相同的原语集，但去除了上下文中的使用示例（即文档字符串中的“示例：”部分）。S1和S2层则基于由这些基础原语组合而成的高级抽象进行操作。


---

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"""Run SAM3 segmentation on an RGB image, optionally conditioned on an image
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"""在 RGB 图像上运行 SAM3 分割，可选择以图像


coordinate point prompt.
坐标点作为提示。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Args:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;参数：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;rgb:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;rgb:


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RGB image array of shape (H, W, 3), dtype uint8.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;形状为 (H, W, 3) 的 RGB 图像数组，数据类型为 uint8。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;point_coords:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;point_coords：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;$\left( {x,y}\right)$ pixel coordinates of the point prompt.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;$\left( {x,y}\right)$ 点提示的像素坐标。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Returns:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;返回：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;masks:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;masks：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A list of dictionaries. Each dict may contain:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;字典列表。每个字典可能包含：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "mask": np.ndarray of shape (H, W), dtype bool or uint8,
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "mask": 形状为 (H, W) 的 np.ndarray，数据类型为 bool 或 uint8，


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;where True/1 means the pixel belongs to the instance.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;其中 True/1 表示像素属于该实例。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "score": float confidence score.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "score": 浮点型置信度分数。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;示例：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;>>> rgb = obs["robot0_robotview"]["images"]["rgb"]
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;>>> rgb = obs["robot0_robotview"]["images"]["rgb"]


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;>>> masks = segment_sam3_point_prompt(rgb, (100, 100))
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;>>> masks = segment_sam3_point_prompt(rgb, (100, 100))


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"""



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return self.sam3_point_prompt_fn(Image.fromarray(rgb), point_coords)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return self.sam3_point_prompt_fn(Image.fromarray(rgb), point_coords)

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RGB image array of shape (H, W, 3), dtype uint8.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;形状为 (H, W, 3)、数据类型为 uint8 的 RGB 图像数组。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;text_prompt:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;text_prompt：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Text prompt for SAMB segmentation.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;用于 SAMB 分割的文本提示。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Returns:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;返回：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;masks:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;masks：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A list of dictionaries. Each dict may contain:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;字典列表。每个字典可能包含：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "mask": np.ndarray of shape $\left( {H,W}\right)$ ,dtype bool or uint8,
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "mask": 形状为 $\left( {H,W}\right)$、数据类型为 bool 或 uint8 的 np.ndarray，


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;where True/1 means the pixel belongs to the instance.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;其中 True/1 表示像素属于该实例。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "box": list [x1, y1, x2, y2] in pixel coordinates.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "box": 像素坐标下的列表 [x1, y1, x2, y2]。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "score": float confidence score.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- "score": 浮点型置信度分数。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;示例：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;>>> rgb = obs["robot0_robotview"]["images"]["rgb"]
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;>>> rgb = obs["robot0_robotview"]["images"]["rgb"]


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;>>> masks = segment_sam3(rgb, text_prompt="red mug")
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;>>> masks = segment_sam3(rgb, text_prompt="red mug")


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"""



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return self.sam3_seg_fn(rgb, text_prompt=text_prompt)

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;若解析失败则返回 (None, None)。

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"""Plan grasp candidates using Contact-GraspNet for a single instance.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"""使用 Contact-GraspNet 为单个实例规划抓取候选点。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This is a thin wrapper around the Contact-GraspNet planner. It does not
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;这是 Contact-GraspNet 规划器的轻量封装，不包含


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;apply any camera/world transforms or TCP offsets: the caller is
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;应用任何相机/世界坐标变换或 TCP 偏移：调用者需


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;responsible for transforming the resulting grasp poses into the des
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;负责将生成的抓取位姿变换至目标坐标系，


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;frame and applying TCP offsets if necessary.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;并在必要时应用 TCP 偏移。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Args:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;参数：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;depth:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;depth：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Depth image in meters.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;深度图像，单位为米。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Shape: (H, W) or (H, W, 1), dtype float32/float64.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;形状：(H, W) 或 (H, W, 1)，数据类型 float32/float64。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;intrinsics:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;intrinsics：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Camera intrinsic matrix.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;相机内参矩阵。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Shape: (3, 3), dtype float64.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;形状：(3, 3)，数据类型 float64。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;segmentation:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;segmentation：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Instance segmentation map where each integer $> 0$ corresponds to a
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;实例分割图，其中每个整数 $> 0$ 对应一个


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;unique object instance ID.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;唯一的物体实例 ID。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Shape: (H, W) or (H, W, 1), dtype int32/int64.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;形状：(H, W) 或 (H, W, 1)，数据类型 int32/int64。

def rotation_matrix_to_quaternion(R: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
def rotation_matrix_to_quaternion(R: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Convert a 3x3 rotation matrix to a unit quaternion $\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{w},\mathrm{x},\mathrm{y},\mathrm{z}}\right\rbrack$ .
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;将 3x3 旋转矩阵转换为单位四元数 $\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{w},\mathrm{x},\mathrm{y},\mathrm{z}}\right\rbrack$ 。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Implements the robust Sheppard's method (checking trace and diagonal elements)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;实现稳健的谢泼德（Sheppard）方法（检查迹和对角元素）


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to avoid numerical instability when the trace is close to zero.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;以避免迹接近零时的数值不稳定。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Args:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;参数：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;R: (3, 3) rotation matrix.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;R: (3, 3) 旋转矩阵。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Returns:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;返回：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;np.array: [w, x, y, z] unit quaternion.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;np.array: [w, x, y, z] 单位四元数。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"""



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;tr = np.trace(R)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;tr = np.trace(R)


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if tr > 0:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if tr > 0:


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;S = np.sqrt(tr + 1.0) * 2
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;S = np.sqrt(tr + 1.0) * 2

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;elif (R[0, 0] > R[1, 1]) and (R[0, 0] > R[2, 2]):
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;elif (R[0, 0] > R[1, 1]) and (R[0, 0] > R[2, 2]):

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;elif R[1, 1] > R[2, 2]:

def transform_points(points: np.ndarray, transform_matrix: np.ndarray) -> np.
def transform_points(points: np.ndarray, transform_matrix: np.ndarray) -> np.


ndarray:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"""

---



&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Apply a 4x4 homogeneous transform to a set of 3D points.

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#转换为齐次坐标 (N, 4)


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ones = np.ones((points_reshaped.shape[0], 1))
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ones = np.ones((points_reshaped.shape[0], 1))


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;points_hom = np.hstack((points_reshaped, ones))
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;points_hom = np.hstack((points_reshaped, ones))


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#Apply transform: $\left( {4,4}\right)$ @ $\left( {4,N}\right)  \rightarrow  \left( {4,N}\right)  \rightarrow$ Transpose back to $\left( {N,4}\right)$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#应用变换：$\left( {4,4}\right)$ @ $\left( {4,N}\right)  \rightarrow  \left( {4,N}\right)  \rightarrow$ 转置回 $\left( {N,4}\right)$


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;points_transformed = (transform_matrix @ points_hom.T).T
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;points_transformed = (transform_matrix @ points_hom.T).T


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#Return to (N, 3) and original shape
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#恢复为 (N, 3) 及原始形状


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return points_transformed[:, :3].reshape(original_shape)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return points_transformed[:, :3].reshape(original_shape)

### G.2. Model Ensemble Temperature Details
### G.2. 模型集成温度设置详情


In both single and multi-model settings, 9 candidates responses are generated. For single model, we query Gemini-3-Pro 9 times with temperatures 0.1, 0.2, 0.3,..., 0.9. For multi-model, we query Gemini-3-Pro, Claude-Opus-4.5, and GPT-5.2 3 times each with temperatures 0.1, 0.5, and 0.9.
在单模型和多模型设置中，均生成 9 个候选响应。对于单模型，我们以 0.1, 0.2, 0.3, ..., 0.9 的温度对 Gemini-3-Pro 进行 9 次查询。对于多模型，我们分别以 0.1, 0.5 和 0.9 的温度对 Gemini-3-Pro、Claude-Opus-4.5 和 GPT-5.2 各进行 3 次查询。

### G.3. 模型集成提示词

你正在将 \{# of candidate generations\} 个候选 Python 解决方案合成为

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SYNTHESIS RULES:
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;合成规则：


1. Analyze critically and assume no candidate is fully correct
1. 批判性分析，假设没有候选方案是完全正确的


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2. Prefer explicit checks over assumptions
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2. 优先使用显式检查而非假设

solution.
解决方案。

### G.4. Multi-turn prompt incentivizing debugging
### G.4. 激励调试的多轮提示词


We noticed that one failure case was inaccurate verification of task completion. Therefore, we experimented with a modified multi-turn prompt which incentivizes verification and debugging, however this did not empirically improve success rate.
我们注意到一种失败情况是任务完成验证不准确。因此，我们尝试了一种改进的多轮提示词，旨在激励验证和调试，但实验结果表明这并未提升成功率。

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- - 若任务未经验证完成：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1. Identify specific bugs, failures, missing steps, or incorrect assumptions.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1. 识别具体的错误、故障、缺失步骤或错误的假设。


---

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2. 解释每个问题为何导致任务无法完成，并引用来自


stdout, stderr, or code behavior.
标准输出、标准错误或代码行为。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3. If the same approach has been attempted multiple times without success, you
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3. 如果同一方法已多次尝试仍未成功，请你


MUST try a fundamentally different strategy.
必须尝试一种根本不同的策略。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4. Brainstorm multiple strategies to fix or verify these issues in the next
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4. 构思多种策略，以便在下一步中修复或验证这些问题


code generation.
代码生成。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5. Synthesize your brainstorming into a single improved Python program that
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5. 将你的头脑风暴整合为一个改进后的 Python 程序，


addresses all identified issues and verifiably completes the task.
解决所有已发现的问题并可验证地完成任务。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6. Respond with the single word 'REGENERATE' followed immediately by new
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6. 回复单词“REGENERATE”，并紧随其后提供新的


Python code in a fenced code block (```python...```)
Python 代码块（```python...```）。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If you choose to regenerate code, you must include your reasoning process only
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;如果你选择重新生成代码，必须仅在代码开头以注释形式


AS COMMENTS at the start of the code explaining:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- What strategies/APIs have already been tried and why they were insufficient

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;重申，你必须仅回复以下选项中的“恰好一个”：


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- The word 'FINISH' if you decide to stop generating code
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- 如果决定停止生成代码，回复单词“FINISH”

### G.5. Model Ensemble Decreases Average Turn Count
### G.5. 模型集成降低了平均轮次


We observed that applying a model ensemble for code generations decreases the average turn count. We noticed that M4 tends to retroactively implement bug fixes and API fallbacks, while the model ensemble preemptively anticipates failures beforehand, resulting in more robust code and lower turn count. See Appendix E.2.4 for a case study on retroactive vs preemptive behavior.
我们观察到，将模型集成应用于代码生成可以降低平均轮次。我们注意到 M4 倾向于事后实施错误修复和 API 回退，而模型集成则能预先规避故障，从而生成更稳健的代码并减少轮次。关于事后行为与预先行为的案例研究，请参阅附录 E.2.4。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_49.jpg?x=514&y=1004&w=727&h=543&r=0"/>



Figure 23. CaP-Agent0 decreases average turn count compared to M4
图 23. 与 M4 相比，CaP-Agent0 降低了平均轮次

## H. 精选案例研究 - 完整生成代码

f place_at_position(position, height_offset=0.05) :
f place_at_position(position, height_offset=0.05) :


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Place currently held object at a specific world position.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;将当前抓取的物体放置在特定的世界坐标位置。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Target orientation is usually top-down (gripper pointing down).
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;目标朝向通常为自上而下（夹爪朝下）。

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#Standard top-down orientation (gripper pointing -z)
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#标准的自上而下朝向（夹爪指向-z轴）


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#A common quaternion for top-down is pointing down z-axis.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#一种常见的自上而下四元数是指向z轴负方向。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#Let's assume the current grasp orientation is maintained or we define a fixed top
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#假设保持当前的抓取朝向，或者定义一个固定的自上而下


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;-down.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;-	朝向。


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#For simplicity, we often maintain the orientation we picked with, or reset to a
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#为简化起见，我们通常保持抓取时的朝向，或重置为


&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;known neutral top-down.
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;已知的标准自上而下朝向。


#Here, we will define a fixed top-down orientation [0, 1, 0, 0] (x-axis rotation
#在此，我们将定义一个固定的自上而下朝向 [0, 1, 0, 0]（x轴旋转

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;180 deg) or similar.

### H.3. Additional Analysis Plots
### H.3. 补充分析图表


We perform additional quantitative analysis on the cube stack task to understand the impact of multi-turn on success rate. We focus our analysis on Gemini 3 Pro (Google DeepMind, 2025), GPT 5.2 (OpenAI, 2025b), and Claude Opus 4.5 (Anthropic, 2025b), the three strongest performers on CaP-Bench. In particular, we plot the probability density function (PDF) of success over turns (Figure 24), PDF of success over tokens (Figure 25), multi-turn success rate vs turn for the cube stacking task in Figure 26. We find that for the cube stacking task, these models would perform the task on the first try, and use the subsequent turns for recovery. Successes for GPT 5.2 and Claude Opus 4.5 seem to have shorter code length than that of Gemini 3 Pro.
我们对立方体堆叠任务进行了额外的定量分析，以了解多轮对话对成功率的影响。分析重点关注 CaP-Bench 上表现最强的三个模型：Gemini 3 Pro (Google DeepMind, 2025)、GPT 5.2 (OpenAI, 2025b) 和 Claude Opus 4.5 (Anthropic, 2025b)。具体而言，我们绘制了成功率随轮次变化的概率密度函数 (PDF)（图 24）、成功率随 Token 变化的 PDF（图 25），以及立方体堆叠任务中多轮成功率与轮次的关系图（图 26）。我们发现，对于立方体堆叠任务，这些模型通常在第一次尝试时就能完成任务，并将后续轮次用于纠错。GPT 5.2 和 Claude Opus 4.5 的成功代码长度似乎比 Gemini 3 Pro 更短。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_55.jpg?x=160&y=1397&w=692&h=427&r=0"/>



Figure 24. Distribution of multi-turn cube stack successes over turns. Results are averaged across M1, M2, and M3.
图 24. 多轮立方体堆叠成功率随轮次的分布。结果为 M1、M2 和 M3 的平均值。


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_55.jpg?x=905&y=1407&w=689&h=431&r=0"/>



Figure 25. Distribution of cube stack successes (S1) over tokens
图 25. 立方体堆叠成功率 (S1) 随 Token 的分布


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/bo_d7pk5ac91nqc7385sok0_56.jpg?x=157&y=187&w=696&h=421&r=0"/>



Figure 26. Cube stack multi-turn success rate vs. turns. Trials with too few or too many turns have lower success rate. Results are averaged across M1, M2, and M3.
图 26. 立方体堆叠多轮成功率与轮次的关系。轮次过少或过多的试验成功率较低。结果为 M1、M2 和 M3 的平均值。


## I. LIBERO-PRO Evaluation Results
## I. LIBERO-PRO 评估结果


We present detailed task-wise performance of OpenVLA, ${\pi }_{0},{\pi }_{0.5}$ ,and CaP-Agent0 on LIBERO-PRO,which evaluates model generalization under initial position perturbations (Pos) and instruction perturbations (Task). Results are summarized in Table 6, Table 7 and Table 8. Each task was executed over 50 trials. In these tasks, CaP-Agent0 struggles with failures in perception, grasp generation, control APIs. For example, queries of "alphabet soup can" to SAM 3 often results in segmentations of the "tomato sauce can" also present in the scene. Also due to the occluded nature of these scenes and the camera not being top down, many grasps generated on desired objects will be at an angle, this, when combined with the lack of collision-aware motion planning often results in other objects in the scene being knocked over during execution, preventing a secure grasp on the desired object.
我们展示了 OpenVLA、${\pi }_{0},{\pi }_{0.5}$ 和 CaP-Agent0 在 LIBERO-PRO 上的详细任务表现，该基准评估了模型在初始位置扰动 (Pos) 和指令扰动 (Task) 下的泛化能力。结果汇总于表 6、表 7 和表 8 中。每项任务均进行了 50 次试验。在这些任务中，CaP-Agent0 在感知、抓取生成和控制 API 方面存在困难。例如，向 SAM 3 查询“字母汤罐头”时，往往会将场景中同时存在的“番茄酱罐头”也一并分割。此外，由于场景存在遮挡且摄像机并非俯视视角，生成的许多目标物体抓取角度倾斜；当结合缺乏碰撞感知的运动规划时，执行过程中常会导致场景中的其他物体被撞倒，从而无法稳固地抓取目标物体。


Table 6. Task-wise LIBERO-PRO performance of OpenVLA, ${\pi }_{0},{\pi }_{0.5}$ and CaP-Agent0 on the libero-object benchmark. Action notation: Place(obj, loc) = pick up object obj and place obj into/onto target loc.
表 6. OpenVLA、${\pi }_{0},{\pi }_{0.5}$ 和 CaP-Agent0 在 libero-object 基准上的 LIBERO-PRO 任务表现。动作符号：Place(obj, loc) = 拾取物体 obj 并将其放置到目标位置 loc。
